// === FILE: nc-ai/cortex/benchmark.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NOVA Benchmark Suite — Written in NC
//  Neural Optimized Vector Architecture
//  Load Testing & Performance Benchmarks
//  Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service "nova-benchmark"
version "1.0.0"

configure:
    port is 8600
    default_iterations is 100
    warmup_iterations is 10

to init:
    purpose: "Initialize benchmark service configuration, defaults, and thresholds"

    // Benchmark Defaults
    set sequence_lengths to [32, 64, 128, 256, 512, 1024]
    set concurrency_levels to [10, 50, 100, 500]
    set sustained_test_duration to 60

    // Model Sizes for Comparison
    set model_sizes to [
        { name: "Micro",  params: "15M",   layers: 6,  hidden: 384,  heads: 6  },
        { name: "Small",  params: "85M",   layers: 12, hidden: 768,  heads: 12 },
        { name: "Base",   params: "250M",  layers: 24, hidden: 1024, heads: 16 },
        { name: "Large",  params: "750M",  layers: 36, hidden: 1536, heads: 24 },
        { name: "1B",     params: "1.3B",  layers: 48, hidden: 2048, heads: 32 },
        { name: "7B",     params: "7B",    layers: 64, hidden: 4096, heads: 32 },
        { name: "20B",    params: "20B",   layers: 96, hidden: 6144, heads: 48 }
    ]

    // LLM Baselines for Comparison (typical values in ms)
    set llm_baselines to {
        forward_ms:  350,
        generate_ms: 1200,
        graph_ms:    150,
        template_ms: 80,
        hebbian_ms:  500
    }

    // Pass/Fail Thresholds
    set thresholds to {
        forward_max_ms:  50,
        generate_max_ms: 200,
        graph_max_ms:    20
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  STATISTICS HELPERS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to calculate_stats with timings:
    sort timings ascending
    set count to length of timings
    set total to 0

    repeat for each t in timings:
        set total to total + t

    set avg to total / count
    set min_val to timings[0]
    set max_val to timings[count - 1]

    set p95_index to math.floor(count * 0.95)
    set p99_index to math.floor(count * 0.99)
    if p95_index is at least count:
        set p95_index to count - 1
    if p99_index is at least count:
        set p99_index to count - 1

    set p95 to timings[p95_index]
    set p99 to timings[p99_index]

    respond with {
        min:   math.round(min_val, 3),
        max:   math.round(max_val, 3),
        avg:   math.round(avg, 3),
        p95:   math.round(p95, 3),
        p99:   math.round(p99, 3),
        count: count
    }

to warmup with model, seq_len:
    log "[NOVA Benchmark] Warming up model with seq_len={seq_len}..."
    set _wi to 0
    repeat while _wi is below warmup_iterations:
        set dummy_input to generate_random_tokens(seq_len)
        call inference.forward_pass with model, dummy_input
        set _wi to _wi + 1
    log "[NOVA Benchmark] Warmup complete."

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  INFERENCE BENCHMARKS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to benchmark_forward_pass with model, iterations:
    set results to []

    repeat for each seq_len in sequence_lengths:
        call warmup with model, seq_len
        set timings to []

        set _it to 0
        repeat while _it is below iterations:
            set input_tokens to generate_random_tokens(seq_len)
            set start to time.now_ms()
            call inference.forward_pass with model, input_tokens
            set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
            append elapsed to timings
            set _it to _it + 1

        set stats to calculate_stats(timings)
        set stats.seq_len to seq_len
        append stats to results
        log "[NOVA] Forward pass seq_len={seq_len}: avg={stats.avg}ms p99={stats.p99}ms"

    respond with results

to benchmark_token_generation with model, iterations:
    set timings to []
    set total_tokens to 0
    set prompt to generate_random_tokens(64)

    call warmup with model, 64

    set _it to 0
    repeat while _it is below iterations:
        set start to time.now_ms()
        set result_data to inference.generate with model, prompt, max_tokens: 128
        set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
        set tokens_generated to length of result_data.tokens
        set total_tokens to total_tokens + tokens_generated
        append elapsed to timings
        set _it to _it + 1

    set stats to calculate_stats(timings)
    set total_time_sec to (math.sum(timings)) / 1000
    set tokens_per_sec to math.round(total_tokens / total_time_sec, 2)

    respond with {
        latency: stats,
        tokens_per_sec: tokens_per_sec,
        total_tokens: total_tokens
    }

to benchmark_graph_query with model, iterations:
    set timings to []

    call warmup with model, 32

    set _it to 0
    repeat while _it is below iterations:
        set query to generate_random_graph_query()
        set start to time.now_ms()
        call CORTEX.graph_query with model, query
        set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
        append elapsed to timings
        set _it to _it + 1

    set stats to calculate_stats(timings)
    log "[NOVA] Graph query: avg={stats.avg}ms p99={stats.p99}ms"
    respond with stats

to benchmark_template_rendering with model, iterations:
    set timings to []
    set templates to [
        "Summarize the following: {input}",
        "Translate to formal tone: {input}",
        "Extract entities from: {input}",
        "Answer the question: {input} Context: {context}",
        "Generate code for: {input} Language: {lang}"
    ]

    set _it to 0
    repeat while _it is below iterations:
        repeat for each tmpl in templates:
            set start to time.now_ms()
            call CORTEX.render_template with model, tmpl, { input: "sample text", context: "ctx", lang: "python" }
            set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
            append elapsed to timings
        set _it to _it + 1

    set stats to calculate_stats(timings)
    log "[NOVA] Template rendering: avg={stats.avg}ms p99={stats.p99}ms"
    respond with stats

to benchmark_hebbian_learning with model, iterations:
    set timings to []
    set sample_data to data.load_sample_batch(batch_size: 32)

    set _it to 0
    repeat while _it is below iterations:
        set start to time.now_ms()
        call train.hebbian_update with model, sample_data
        set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
        append elapsed to timings
        set _it to _it + 1

    set stats to calculate_stats(timings)
    log "[NOVA] Hebbian learning: avg={stats.avg}ms p99={stats.p99}ms"
    respond with stats

to run_inference_benchmarks with options:
    set model to inference.load_model(options.model_name or "nova-base")
    set iterations to options.iterations or default_iterations

    log "============================================="
    log "  NOVA Inference Benchmark Suite"
    log "  Model: {options.model_name or 'nova-base'}"
    log "  Iterations: {iterations}"
    log "============================================="

    set forward_results to benchmark_forward_pass(model, iterations)
    set generation_results to benchmark_token_generation(model, iterations)
    set graph_results to benchmark_graph_query(model, iterations)
    set template_results to benchmark_template_rendering(model, iterations)
    set hebbian_results to benchmark_hebbian_learning(model, iterations)

    respond with {
        type:       "inference",
        model:      options.model_name or "nova-base",
        iterations: iterations,
        timestamp:  time.now_iso(),
        results: {
            forward_pass:       forward_results,
            token_generation:   generation_results,
            graph_query:        graph_results,
            template_rendering: template_results,
            hebbian_learning:   hebbian_results
        }
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  LOAD TESTING
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to simulate_single_request with model:
    set request_type to math.random_choice(["forward", "generate", "graph", "template"])
    set start to time.now_ms()

    if request_type is "forward":
        set input to generate_random_tokens(128)
        call inference.forward_pass with model, input
    if request_type is "generate":
        set prompt to generate_random_tokens(32)
        call inference.generate with model, prompt, max_tokens: 64
    if request_type is "graph":
        set query to generate_random_graph_query()
        call CORTEX.graph_query with model, query
    if request_type is "template":
        call CORTEX.render_template with model, "Summarize: {input}", { input: "benchmark text" }

    set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
    respond with { type: request_type, latency_ms: elapsed }

to benchmark_concurrent with model, num_concurrent:
    log "[NOVA Load] Testing {num_concurrent} concurrent requests..."
    set tasks to []
    set start to time.now_ms()

    set _nc to 0
    repeat while _nc is below num_concurrent:
        set task to async simulate_single_request(model)
        append task to tasks
        set _nc to _nc + 1

    set results to await_all(tasks)
    set total_elapsed to time.now_ms() - start

    set latencies to []
    repeat for each r in results:
        append r.latency_ms to latencies

    set stats to calculate_stats(latencies)

    respond with {
        concurrency:    num_concurrent,
        total_time_ms:  total_elapsed,
        latency:        stats,
        requests_per_sec: math.round((num_concurrent / total_elapsed) * 1000, 2)
    }

to benchmark_sustained_throughput with model, duration_sec:
    log "[NOVA Load] Sustained throughput test for {duration_sec}s..."
    set start to time.now_ms()
    set end_time to start + (duration_sec * 1000)
    set request_count to 0
    set latencies to []
    set memory_snapshots to []
    set second_counts to []
    set current_second to 0

    repeat while time.now_ms() is below end_time:
        set req_start to time.now_ms()
        call simulate_single_request with model
        set req_elapsed to time.now_ms() - req_start
        append req_elapsed to latencies
        set request_count to request_count + 1

        set elapsed_seconds to math.floor((time.now_ms() - start) / 1000)
        if elapsed_seconds is above current_second:
            append { second: current_second, count: request_count } to second_counts
            append system.memory_usage_mb() to memory_snapshots
            set current_second to elapsed_seconds

    set total_elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
    set stats to calculate_stats(latencies)

    respond with {
        duration_sec:     duration_sec,
        total_requests:   request_count,
        total_time_ms:    total_elapsed,
        requests_per_sec: math.round((request_count / total_elapsed) * 1000, 2),
        latency:          stats,
        memory_snapshots: memory_snapshots,
        throughput_by_second: second_counts
    }

to track_memory_under_load with model, num_requests:
    log "[NOVA Load] Tracking memory across {num_requests} requests..."
    set memory_before to system.memory_usage_mb()
    set peak_memory to memory_before
    set samples to []

    set i to 0
    repeat while i is below num_requests:
        call simulate_single_request with model
        set current_mem to system.memory_usage_mb()
        if current_mem is above peak_memory:
            set peak_memory to current_mem
        if (i % 50) is 0:
            append { request: i, memory_mb: current_mem } to samples
        set i to i + 1

    set memory_after to system.memory_usage_mb()

    respond with {
        memory_before_mb: memory_before,
        memory_after_mb:  memory_after,
        peak_memory_mb:   peak_memory,
        delta_mb:         math.round(memory_after - memory_before, 2),
        samples:          samples
    }

to run_load_benchmarks with options:
    set model to inference.load_model(options.model_name or "nova-base")

    log "============================================="
    log "  NOVA Load Testing Suite"
    log "  Model: {options.model_name or 'nova-base'}"
    log "============================================="

    set concurrency_results to []
    repeat for each level in concurrency_levels:
        set result to benchmark_concurrent(model, level)
        append result to concurrency_results

    set sustained_result to benchmark_sustained_throughput(model, sustained_test_duration)
    set memory_result to track_memory_under_load(model, 500)

    respond with {
        type:       "load",
        model:      options.model_name or "nova-base",
        timestamp:  time.now_iso(),
        results: {
            concurrency:          concurrency_results,
            sustained_throughput: sustained_result,
            memory_tracking:      memory_result
        }
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  MODEL SIZE COMPARISON
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to run_model_comparison with options:
    set iterations to options.iterations or 50
    set comparison_results to []

    log "============================================="
    log "  NOVA Model Size Comparison"
    log "  Iterations per size: {iterations}"
    log "============================================="

    repeat for each size in model_sizes:
        log "[NOVA] Benchmarking model size: {size.name} ({size.params} params)..."

        try:
            set model to inference.load_model("nova-{lowercase(size.name)}")
            set mem_before to system.memory_usage_mb()

            // Forward pass
            set fwd_timings to []
            set _fi to 0
            repeat while _fi is below iterations:
                set input to generate_random_tokens(128)
                set start to time.now_ms()
                call inference.forward_pass with model, input
                set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
                append elapsed to fwd_timings
                set _fi to _fi + 1

            // Token generation
            set gen_timings to []
            set _gi to 0
            repeat while _gi is below iterations:
                set prompt to generate_random_tokens(32)
                set start to time.now_ms()
                call inference.generate with model, prompt, max_tokens: 64
                set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
                append elapsed to gen_timings
                set _gi to _gi + 1

            // Graph query
            set graph_timings to []
            set _gqi to 0
            repeat while _gqi is below iterations:
                set query to generate_random_graph_query()
                set start to time.now_ms()
                call CORTEX.graph_query with model, query
                set elapsed to time.now_ms() - start
                append elapsed to graph_timings
                set _gqi to _gqi + 1

            set mem_after to system.memory_usage_mb()

            set entry to {
                name:        size.name,
                params:      size.params,
                layers:      size.layers,
                hidden:      size.hidden,
                heads:       size.heads,
                memory_mb:   math.round(mem_after - mem_before, 2),
                forward_ms:  calculate_stats(fwd_timings).avg,
                generate_ms: calculate_stats(gen_timings).avg,
                graph_ms:    calculate_stats(graph_timings).avg
            }
            append entry to comparison_results
            log "[NOVA] {size.name}: fwd={entry.forward_ms}ms gen={entry.generate_ms}ms graph={entry.graph_ms}ms mem={entry.memory_mb}MB"

        on error:
            log "[NOVA] Skipped {size.name}: load failed"
            append { name: size.name, params: size.params, error: "load failed" } to comparison_results

    respond with {
        type:       "comparison",
        iterations: iterations,
        timestamp:  time.now_iso(),
        results:    comparison_results
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  LLM BASELINE COMPARISON
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to run_baseline_comparison with options:
    set model to inference.load_model(options.model_name or "nova-base")
    set iterations to options.iterations or default_iterations

    log "============================================="
    log "  NOVA vs LLM Baseline Comparison"
    log "  Model: {options.model_name or 'nova-base'}"
    log "============================================="

    // Run NOVA benchmarks
    set fwd_timings to []
    set gen_timings to []
    set graph_timings to []
    set tmpl_timings to []
    set hebb_timings to []

    call warmup with model, 128

    set _it to 0
    repeat while _it is below iterations:
        set input to generate_random_tokens(128)

        set start to time.now_ms()
        call inference.forward_pass with model, input
        append (time.now_ms() - start) to fwd_timings

        set start to time.now_ms()
        call inference.generate with model, input, max_tokens: 64
        append (time.now_ms() - start) to gen_timings

        set start to time.now_ms()
        call CORTEX.graph_query with model, generate_random_graph_query()
        append (time.now_ms() - start) to graph_timings

        set start to time.now_ms()
        call CORTEX.render_template with model, "Summarize: {input}", { input: "text" }
        append (time.now_ms() - start) to tmpl_timings

        set start to time.now_ms()
        call train.hebbian_update with model, data.load_sample_batch(batch_size: 16)
        append (time.now_ms() - start) to hebb_timings
        set _it to _it + 1

    set nova_results to {
        forward_ms:  calculate_stats(fwd_timings).avg,
        generate_ms: calculate_stats(gen_timings).avg,
        graph_ms:    calculate_stats(graph_timings).avg,
        template_ms: calculate_stats(tmpl_timings).avg,
        hebbian_ms:  calculate_stats(hebb_timings).avg
    }

    set comparisons to []

    repeat for each key in ["forward_ms", "generate_ms", "graph_ms", "template_ms", "hebbian_ms"]:
        set nova_val to nova_results[key]
        set llm_val to llm_baselines[key]
        set speedup to math.round(llm_val / nova_val, 2)
        append {
            metric:          key,
            nova_ms:         nova_val,
            llm_baseline_ms: llm_val,
            speedup:         speedup,
            faster:          nova_val is below llm_val
        } to comparisons

    respond with {
        type:       "baseline_comparison",
        model:      options.model_name or "nova-base",
        iterations: iterations,
        timestamp:  time.now_iso(),
        nova:       nova_results,
        baselines:  llm_baselines,
        comparisons: comparisons
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  REPORT GENERATION
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to generate_report with all_results:
    set lines to []

    append "================================================================" to lines
    append "  NOVA BENCHMARK REPORT" to lines
    append "  Neural Optimized Vector Architecture" to lines
    append "  Generated: {time.now_iso()}" to lines
    append "  Version: {nova_version}" to lines
    append "================================================================" to lines
    append "" to lines

    // Inference Results
    if all_results.inference is not nothing:
        set inf to all_results.inference
        append "--- INFERENCE BENCHMARKS ---" to lines
        append "Model: {inf.model}  |  Iterations: {inf.iterations}" to lines
        append "" to lines

        append "  Forward Pass Latency:" to lines
        append "  +-----------+----------+----------+----------+----------+----------+" to lines
        append "  | Seq Len   | Min (ms) | Avg (ms) | Max (ms) | P95 (ms) | P99 (ms) |" to lines
        append "  +-----------+----------+----------+----------+----------+----------+" to lines
        repeat for each r in inf.results.forward_pass:
            set line to "  | {pad_right(r.seq_len, 9)} | {pad_right(r.min, 8)} | {pad_right(r.avg, 8)} | {pad_right(r.max, 8)} | {pad_right(r.p95, 8)} | {pad_right(r.p99, 8)} |"
            append line to lines
        append "  +-----------+----------+----------+----------+----------+----------+" to lines
        append "" to lines

        set gen to inf.results.token_generation
        append "  Token Generation:" to lines
        append "    Throughput:  {gen.tokens_per_sec} tokens/sec" to lines
        append "    Avg Latency: {gen.latency.avg} ms" to lines
        append "    P99 Latency: {gen.latency.p99} ms" to lines
        append "" to lines

        set gq to inf.results.graph_query
        append "  Graph Query:       avg={gq.avg}ms  p95={gq.p95}ms  p99={gq.p99}ms" to lines

        set tr to inf.results.template_rendering
        append "  Template Render:   avg={tr.avg}ms  p95={tr.p95}ms  p99={tr.p99}ms" to lines

        set hb to inf.results.hebbian_learning
        append "  Hebbian Learning:  avg={hb.avg}ms  p95={hb.p95}ms  p99={hb.p99}ms" to lines
        append "" to lines

    // Load Results
    if all_results.load is not nothing:
        set ld to all_results.load
        append "--- LOAD TEST RESULTS ---" to lines
        append "" to lines

        append "  Concurrency Tests:" to lines
        append "  +-------------+------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+" to lines
        append "  | Concurrency | Total (ms) | Avg (ms)  | P99 (ms)  | Req/sec   |" to lines
        append "  +-------------+------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+" to lines
        repeat for each c in ld.results.concurrency:
            set line to "  | {pad_right(c.concurrency, 11)} | {pad_right(c.total_time_ms, 10)} | {pad_right(c.latency.avg, 9)} | {pad_right(c.latency.p99, 9)} | {pad_right(c.requests_per_sec, 9)} |"
            append line to lines
        append "  +-------------+------------+-----------+-----------+-----------+" to lines
        append "" to lines

        set st to ld.results.sustained_throughput
        append "  Sustained Throughput ({st.duration_sec}s):" to lines
        append "    Total Requests:  {st.total_requests}" to lines
        append "    Requests/sec:    {st.requests_per_sec}" to lines
        append "    Avg Latency:     {st.latency.avg} ms" to lines
        append "    P99 Latency:     {st.latency.p99} ms" to lines
        append "" to lines

        set mem to ld.results.memory_tracking
        append "  Memory Usage:" to lines
        append "    Before: {mem.memory_before_mb} MB" to lines
        append "    After:  {mem.memory_after_mb} MB" to lines
        append "    Peak:   {mem.peak_memory_mb} MB" to lines
        append "    Delta:  {mem.delta_mb} MB" to lines
        append "" to lines

    // Model Comparison
    if all_results.comparison is not nothing:
        set cmp to all_results.comparison
        append "--- MODEL SIZE COMPARISON ---" to lines
        append "" to lines
        append "  +--------+--------+----------+------------+-------------+----------+" to lines
        append "  | Model  | Params | Mem (MB) | Fwd (ms)   | Gen (ms)    | Graph(ms)|" to lines
        append "  +--------+--------+----------+------------+-------------+----------+" to lines
        repeat for each m in cmp.results:
            if m.error is not nothing:
                set line to "  | {pad_right(m.name, 6)} | {pad_right(m.params, 6)} | ERROR: {m.error}"
            else:
                set line to "  | {pad_right(m.name, 6)} | {pad_right(m.params, 6)} | {pad_right(m.memory_mb, 8)} | {pad_right(m.forward_ms, 10)} | {pad_right(m.generate_ms, 11)} | {pad_right(m.graph_ms, 8)} |"
            append line to lines
        append "  +--------+--------+----------+------------+-------------+----------+" to lines
        append "" to lines

    // Baseline Comparison
    if all_results.baseline_comparison is not nothing:
        set bc to all_results.baseline_comparison
        append "--- NOVA vs LLM BASELINES ---" to lines
        append "" to lines
        append "  +----------------+------------+---------------+----------+---------+" to lines
        append "  | Metric         | NOVA (ms)  | LLM Base (ms) | Speedup  | Faster? |" to lines
        append "  +----------------+------------+---------------+----------+---------+" to lines
        repeat for each c in bc.comparisons:
            set faster_str to "YES" if c.faster else "NO"
            set line to "  | {pad_right(c.metric, 14)} | {pad_right(c.nova_ms, 10)} | {pad_right(c.llm_baseline_ms, 13)} | {pad_right(c.speedup, 8)}x| {pad_right(faster_str, 7)} |"
            append line to lines
        append "  +----------------+------------+---------------+----------+---------+" to lines
        append "" to lines

    // Pass/Fail Verdict
    append "--- PASS / FAIL CRITERIA ---" to lines
    append "" to lines

    set all_pass to true

    if all_results.inference is not nothing:
        set fwd_avg to all_results.inference.results.forward_pass[2].avg
        set gen_avg to all_results.inference.results.token_generation.latency.avg
        set grp_avg to all_results.inference.results.graph_query.avg

        set fwd_pass to fwd_avg is below thresholds.forward_max_ms
        set gen_pass to gen_avg is below thresholds.generate_max_ms
        set grp_pass to grp_avg is below thresholds.graph_max_ms

        set fwd_status to "PASS" if fwd_pass else "FAIL"
        set gen_status to "PASS" if gen_pass else "FAIL"
        set grp_status to "PASS" if grp_pass else "FAIL"

        append "  Forward pass (seq 128) < {thresholds.forward_max_ms}ms:   {fwd_avg}ms  [{fwd_status}]" to lines
        append "  Token generation       < {thresholds.generate_max_ms}ms:  {gen_avg}ms  [{gen_status}]" to lines
        append "  Graph query            < {thresholds.graph_max_ms}ms:   {grp_avg}ms  [{grp_status}]" to lines

        if not fwd_pass or not gen_pass or not grp_pass:
            set all_pass to false

    append "" to lines
    set verdict to "ALL BENCHMARKS PASSED" if all_pass else "SOME BENCHMARKS FAILED"
    append "  Verdict: [{verdict}]" to lines
    append "" to lines
    append "================================================================" to lines
    append "  Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI. All rights reserved." to lines
    append "================================================================" to lines

    set report_text to join lines with newline
    respond with { text: report_text, pass: all_pass }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HELPER FUNCTIONS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to generate_random_tokens with length:
    set tokens to []
    set _li to 0
    repeat while _li is below length:
        append math.random_int(1, 50000) to tokens
        set _li to _li + 1
    respond with tokens

to generate_random_graph_query:
    set queries to [
        { type: "neighbor", node_id: math.random_int(1, 10000), depth: 2 },
        { type: "path", from: math.random_int(1, 10000), to: math.random_int(1, 10000) },
        { type: "cluster", node_id: math.random_int(1, 10000), radius: 3 },
        { type: "similarity", embedding: generate_random_tokens(32), top_k: 10 },
        { type: "subgraph", center: math.random_int(1, 10000), hops: 2 }
    ]
    respond with math.random_choice(queries)

to pad_right with value, width:
    set s to to_str(value)
    repeat while len(s) is below width:
        set s to s + " "
    respond with s

to lowercase with text:
    respond with text.to_lower()

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HTTP API ENDPOINTS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to handle_benchmark_all with request:
    set options to request.body or {}
    log "[NOVA] Starting full benchmark suite..."

    set inference_results to run_inference_benchmarks(options)
    set load_results to run_load_benchmarks(options)
    set comparison_results to run_model_comparison(options)
    set baseline_results to run_baseline_comparison(options)

    set all_results to {
        inference:           inference_results,
        load:                load_results,
        comparison:          comparison_results,
        baseline_comparison: baseline_results
    }

    set report to generate_report(all_results)
    log report.text

    respond with {
        status: "complete",
        report: report.text,
        pass:   report.pass,
        data:   all_results
    }

to handle_benchmark_inference with request:
    set options to request.body or {}
    set results to run_inference_benchmarks(options)
    set report to generate_report({ inference: results })

    respond with {
        status: "complete",
        report: report.text,
        pass:   report.pass,
        data:   results
    }

to handle_benchmark_load with request:
    set options to request.body or {}
    set results to run_load_benchmarks(options)
    set report to generate_report({ load: results })

    respond with {
        status: "complete",
        report: report.text,
        data:   results
    }

to handle_benchmark_compare with request:
    set options to request.body or {}
    set comparison to run_model_comparison(options)
    set baseline to run_baseline_comparison(options)

    set report to generate_report({
        comparison:          comparison,
        baseline_comparison: baseline
    })

    respond with {
        status: "complete",
        report: report.text,
        data: {
            model_comparison:    comparison,
            baseline_comparison: baseline
        }
    }

to handle_report with request:
    // Return the last cached report or run a quick benchmark
    if last_report is not nothing:
        respond with { status: "ok", report: last_report.text, pass: last_report.pass }
    else:
        respond with { status: "no_report", message: "No benchmark has been run yet. POST to /benchmark/all first." }

to handle_health with request:
    respond with {
        status:  "healthy",
        service: service_name,
        version: nova_version,
        uptime:  time.uptime_seconds(),
        memory:  system.memory_usage_mb()
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SERVICE STARTUP
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

api:
    POST /benchmark/all       runs handle_benchmark_all
    POST /benchmark/inference runs handle_benchmark_inference
    POST /benchmark/load      runs handle_benchmark_load
    POST /benchmark/compare   runs handle_benchmark_compare
    GET  /report              runs handle_report
    GET  /health              runs handle_health

to start:
    purpose: "Initialize service state and log startup banner"
    set last_report to nothing

    log "================================================================"
    log "  NOVA Benchmark Service"
    log "  Neural Optimized Vector Architecture"
    log "  Version: 1.0.0"
    log ""
    log "  Endpoints:"
    log "    POST /benchmark/all        - Full benchmark suite"
    log "    POST /benchmark/inference  - Inference benchmarks only"
    log "    POST /benchmark/load       - Load testing only"
    log "    POST /benchmark/compare    - Model size & LLM comparison"
    log "    GET  /report               - Last benchmark report"
    log "    GET  /health               - Service health check"
    log ""
    log "  Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI. All rights reserved."
    log "================================================================"

// === FILE: nc-ai/cortex/codegen.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NOVA Code Generation Module — Written in NC
//  Analyzes natural-language prompts and generates complete NC apps.
//  Pipeline:  Prompt → Analyze → Classify → Template → Generate
//  Usage:
//    nc nc-ai/cortex/codegen.nc
//    curl -X POST http://localhost:8900/generate \
//      -d '{"prompt": "build a user management API with auth"}'
//  Patent: DevHeal Labs AI — NOVA Model Architecture
//  Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI. All rights reserved.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
service "nova-codegen"
version "1.0.0"
configure:
    port is 8900
    max_prompt_length is 2000
    default_service_port is 9000
// --- KEYWORD MAPS ---
to init:
    purpose: "Initialize NOVA code generation engine"
    set app_type_keywords to {
        "api":  ["api", "rest", "endpoint", "crud", "service", "server", "backend"],
        "cli":  ["cli", "command", "terminal", "console", "shell", "tool"],
        "web":  ["web", "page", "frontend", "html", "site", "dashboard"],
        "ml":   ["ml", "model", "train", "predict", "classify", "neural", "ai"],
        "data": ["data", "pipeline", "etl", "transform", "csv", "stream", "ingest"]
    }
    set entity_keywords to ["user", "product", "order", "task", "post", "comment", "message", "category", "tag", "role", "session", "payment", "item", "blog", "article", "chat", "notification", "invoice", "customer"]
    set endpoint_verbs to ["create", "read", "update", "delete", "list", "get", "add", "remove", "edit", "fetch", "search", "filter", "upload"]
    log "NOVA codegen service started on port {port}"

// --- 1. PROMPT ANALYSIS ---
to score_type with lower_prompt, type_name:
    set score to 0
    repeat for each kw in app_type_keywords[type_name]:
        set kw_found to lower_prompt contains kw
        if kw_found is true:
            set score to score + 1
    respond with score

to collect_endpoints with lower_prompt, found_entities:
    set found_endpoints to []
    repeat for each ent in found_entities:
        repeat for each verb in endpoint_verbs:
            set verb_found to lower_prompt contains verb
            if verb_found is true:
                append {verb: verb, entity: ent} to found_endpoints
    respond with found_endpoints

to analyze_prompt with prompt:
    set result to {}
    set lower_prompt to lowercase prompt
    set detected_type to "api"
    set best_score to 0
    set type_list to keys app_type_keywords
    repeat for each type_name in type_list:
        set score to score_type with lower_prompt, type_name
        if score is above best_score:
            set best_score to score
            set detected_type to type_name
    set result["app_type"] to detected_type
    set found_entities to []
    repeat for each ent in entity_keywords:
        set ent_found to lower_prompt contains ent
        if ent_found is true:
            append ent to found_entities
    set ent_count to length found_entities
    if ent_count is 0:
        append "item" to found_entities
    set result["entities"] to found_entities
    set result["endpoints"] to collect_endpoints with lower_prompt, found_entities
    set models to []
    repeat for each ent in found_entities:
        append {name: ent, fields: ["id", "name", "created_at", "updated_at"]} to models
    set result["models"] to models
    set result["prompt"] to prompt
    log "NOVA codegen: analyzed — type={detected_type}, entities={found_entities}"
    respond with result

// --- 2. CODE TEMPLATES (6 types) ---
to init_templates:
    purpose: "Initialize code generation templates"
    set t1 to "service \"{{service_name}}\"\nconfigure:\n    port is {{port}}\n"
    set t2 to "set {{entity}}_store to []\nset next_id to 1\n"
    set t3 to "to create_{{entity}} with data:\n    set data[\"id\"] to next_id\n    set data[\"created_at\"] to now()\n    set next_id to next_id + 1\n    append data to {{entity}}_store\n    respond with data\n"
    set t4 to "to list_{{entity}}s:\n    respond with {{entity}}_store\nto get_{{entity}} with id:\n    repeat for each item in {{entity}}_store:\n        if item[\"id\"] is id:\n            respond with item\n    respond with {error: \"not found\"}\n"
    set t5 to "to update_{{entity}} with id, data:\n    repeat for each item in {{entity}}_store:\n        if item[\"id\"] is id:\n            set item[\"name\"] to data[\"name\"]\n            set item[\"updated_at\"] to now()\n            respond with item\n    respond with {error: \"not found\"}\n"
    set t6 to "to delete_{{entity}} with id:\n    set kept to []\n    repeat for each item in {{entity}}_store:\n        if item[\"id\"] is not id:\n            append item to kept\n    set {{entity}}_store to kept\n    respond with {status: \"deleted\"}\n"
    set t7 to "api:\n    POST /{{entity}} runs create_{{entity}}\n    GET /{{entity}}s runs list_{{entity}}s\n    GET /{{entity}}/:id runs get_{{entity}}\n    PUT /{{entity}}/:id runs update_{{entity}}\n    DELETE /{{entity}}/:id runs delete_{{entity}}\n"
    set template_rest_api to t1 + t2 + t3 + t4 + t5 + t6 + t7
    set template_cli_tool to "service \"{{service_name}}\"\nto handle_command with args:\n    set cmd to args[0]\n    if cmd is \"help\":\n        respond with \"Usage: {{service_name}} [create|list|delete]\"\n    if cmd is \"create\":\n        respond with {status: \"created\", name: args[1]}\n    if cmd is \"list\":\n        respond with {status: \"ok\"}\n    if cmd is \"delete\":\n        respond with {status: \"deleted\"}\n    respond with {error: \"unknown command\"}\napi:\n    start runs handle_command\n"
    set a1 to "service \"{{service_name}}-auth\"\nconfigure:\n    port is {{port}}\nset users_store to []\nset sessions to []\n"
    set a2 to "to register_user with data:\n    set user to {id: 1, username: data[\"username\"], created_at: now()}\n    append user to users_store\n    respond with {id: user[\"id\"], username: user[\"username\"]}\n"
    set a3 to "to login_user with creds:\n    repeat for each u in users_store:\n        if u[\"username\"] is creds[\"username\"]:\n            respond with {token: \"token\", expires_in: 3600}\n    respond with {error: \"invalid credentials\"}\n"
    set a4 to "to verify_token with token:\n    respond with {valid: true}\napi:\n    POST /auth/register runs register_user\n    POST /auth/login runs login_user\n    POST /auth/verify runs verify_token\n"
    set template_auth_service to a1 + a2 + a3 + a4
    set d1 to "service \"{{service_name}}-pipeline\"\nconfigure:\n    port is {{port}}\nset pipeline_log to []\n"
    set d2 to "to ingest_data with source:\n    set raw to fetch_data(source[\"uri\"])\n    respond with raw\nto transform_data with data, rules:\n    set result_data to []\n    respond with result_data\n"
    set d3 to "to load_data with data, target:\n    respond with {stage: \"load\", status: \"complete\"}\napi:\n    POST /pipeline/run runs ingest_data\n    GET /pipeline/status runs health\n"
    set template_data_pipeline to d1 + d2 + d3
    set m1 to "service \"{{service_name}}-ml\"\nconfigure:\n    port is {{port}}\nset training_jobs to []\n"
    set m2 to "to train_model with config:\n    set job to {id: 1, status: \"running\", model: config[\"model\"]}\n    append job to training_jobs\n    respond with job\n"
    set m3 to "to predict with model_name, input:\n    respond with {model: model_name, prediction: null}\napi:\n    POST /ml/train runs train_model\n    POST /ml/predict runs predict\n    GET /ml/jobs runs health\n"
    set template_ml_pipeline to m1 + m2 + m3
    set ms1 to "service \"{{service_name}}\"\nconfigure:\n    port is {{port}}\n"
    set ms2 to "to handle_request with action, payload:\n    if action is \"process\":\n        respond with {result: null}\n    respond with {error: \"unknown action\"}\n"
    set ms3 to "api:\n    POST /process runs handle_request\n    GET /health runs health\n"
    set template_microservice to ms1 + ms2 + ms3
// --- 3. GENERATION FUNCTIONS ---
to generate_service with spec:
    set app_type to spec["app_type"]
    set entity to spec["entities"][0]
    set svc_name to spec["service_name"] or entity + "-service"
    set svc_port to spec["port"] or default_service_port
    if app_type is "api":
        set tpl to template_rest_api
    if app_type is "cli":
        set tpl to template_cli_tool
    if app_type is "data":
        set tpl to template_data_pipeline
    if app_type is "ml":
        set tpl to template_ml_pipeline
    if app_type is not "api" and app_type is not "cli" and app_type is not "data" and app_type is not "ml":
        set tpl to template_microservice
    set code to replace tpl "{{service_name}}" with svc_name
    set code to replace code "{{entity}}" with entity
    set code to replace code "{{port}}" with svc_port
    log "NOVA codegen: generated {app_type} — {svc_name}:{svc_port}"
    respond with {code: code, service_name: svc_name, port: svc_port, type: app_type}
to generate_endpoints with entities:
    set all_endpoints to []
    repeat for each ent in entities:
        set b to "on POST \"/" + ent + "\":\n    create_" + ent + " with request.body\n"
        set b to b + "on GET \"/" + ent + "s\":\n    list_" + ent + "s\n"
        set b to b + "on GET \"/" + ent + "/:id\":\n    get_" + ent + " with request.params.id\n"
        set b to b + "on PUT \"/" + ent + "/:id\":\n    update_" + ent + " with request.params.id, request.body\n"
        set b to b + "on DELETE \"/" + ent + "/:id\":\n    delete_" + ent + " with request.params.id\n"
        append {entity: ent, code: b} to all_endpoints
    respond with all_endpoints
to generate_model with name, fields:
    set code to "set " + name + "_schema to {\n"
    repeat for each f in fields:
        set code to code + "    \"" + f + "\": {required: true},\n"
    set code to code + "}\nto validate_" + name + " with data:\n"
    repeat for each f in fields:
        set code to code + "    if data[\"" + f + "\"] is null:\n"
        set code to code + "        respond with {error: \"" + f + " is required\"}\n"
    set code to code + "    respond with {valid: true}\n"
    respond with {name: name, code: code, fields: fields}
to generate_full_app with prompt:
    set analysis to analyze_prompt with prompt
    set entities to analysis["entities"]
    set spec to {app_type: analysis["app_type"], entities: entities, service_name: entities[0] + "-service", port: default_service_port}
    set main_svc to generate_service with spec
    set endpoints to generate_endpoints with entities
    set models to []
    repeat for each m in analysis["models"]:
        set model_item to generate_model with m["name"], m["fields"]
        append model_item to models
    set auth_code to null
    set lp to lowercase prompt
    set needs_auth to lp contains "auth" or lp contains "login" or lp contains "register"
    if needs_auth is true:
        set auth_code to template_auth_service
    log "NOVA codegen: full app — type={analysis['app_type']}, entities={entities}"
    set app_type to analysis["app_type"]
    respond with {prompt: prompt, app_type: app_type, main_service: main_svc, endpoints: endpoints, models: models, auth: auth_code, entities: entities, generated_at: now()}
// --- 4. REAL-WORLD EXAMPLES (5 complete NC apps) ---
to init_examples:
    purpose: "Initialize example NC applications"
    set examples to []
    set ex1_code to "service \"user-mgmt\"\nconfigure:\n    port is 9001\nset users to []\nset nid to 1\nto register with data:\n    set user to {id: nid, name: data[\"name\"], email: data[\"email\"], created_at: now()}\n    set nid to nid + 1\n    append user to users\n    respond with user\nto get_user with id:\n    repeat for each u in users:\n        if u[\"id\"] is id:\n            respond with u\n    respond with {error: \"not found\"}\napi:\n    POST /users runs register\n    GET /users/:id runs get_user\n"
    append {name: "User Management API", prompt: "user management API with auth", code: ex1_code} to examples
    set ex2_code to "service \"ecommerce\"\nconfigure:\n    port is 9002\nset products to []\nset orders to []\nset npid to 1\nset noid to 1\nto add_product with data:\n    set p to {id: npid, name: data[\"name\"], price: data[\"price\"], created_at: now()}\n    set npid to npid + 1\n    append p to products\n    respond with p\nto place_order with data:\n    set order to {id: noid, items: data[\"items\"], status: \"pending\", created_at: now()}\n    set noid to noid + 1\n    append order to orders\n    respond with order\napi:\n    POST /products runs add_product\n    GET /products runs health\n    POST /orders runs place_order\n"
    append {name: "E-commerce Service", prompt: "e-commerce with products and orders", code: ex2_code} to examples
    set ex3_code to "service \"blog-platform\"\nconfigure:\n    port is 9003\nset posts to []\nset comments to []\nset npid to 1\nset ncid to 1\nto create_post with data:\n    set post to {id: npid, title: data[\"title\"], body: data[\"body\"], author: data[\"author\"], created_at: now()}\n    set npid to npid + 1\n    append post to posts\n    respond with post\nto add_comment with post_id, data:\n    set c to {id: ncid, post_id: post_id, author: data[\"author\"], text: data[\"text\"], created_at: now()}\n    set ncid to ncid + 1\n    append c to comments\n    respond with c\napi:\n    POST /posts runs create_post\n    GET /posts runs health\n    POST /posts/:id/comments runs add_comment\n"
    append {name: "Blog Platform", prompt: "blog platform with posts and comments", code: ex3_code} to examples
    set ex4_code to "service \"task-manager\"\nconfigure:\n    port is 9004\nset tasks to []\nset nid to 1\nto create_task with data:\n    set t to {id: nid, title: data[\"title\"], status: \"open\", priority: data[\"priority\"] or \"medium\", created_at: now()}\n    set nid to nid + 1\n    append t to tasks\n    respond with t\nto update_status with id, status:\n    repeat for each t in tasks:\n        if t[\"id\"] is id:\n            set t[\"status\"] to status\n            respond with t\n    respond with {error: \"not found\"}\napi:\n    POST /tasks runs create_task\n    GET /tasks runs health\n    PUT /tasks/:id/status runs update_status\n"
    append {name: "Task Management", prompt: "task management API with assignments", code: ex4_code} to examples
    set ex5_code to "service \"chat-service\"\nconfigure:\n    port is 9005\nset rooms to []\nset messages to []\nset nrid to 1\nset nmid to 1\nto create_room with data:\n    set room to {id: nrid, name: data[\"name\"], members: data[\"members\"] or [], created_at: now()}\n    set nrid to nrid + 1\n    append room to rooms\n    respond with room\nto send_message with room_id, data:\n    set msg to {id: nmid, room_id: room_id, sender: data[\"sender\"], text: data[\"text\"], created_at: now()}\n    set nmid to nmid + 1\n    append msg to messages\n    respond with msg\napi:\n    POST /rooms runs create_room\n    GET /rooms runs health\n    POST /rooms/:id/messages runs send_message\n"
    append {name: "Chat Service", prompt: "chat service with rooms and messages", code: ex5_code} to examples

// --- 5. API ROUTES ---
to handle_generate:
    purpose: "Generate a full NC application from a natural-language prompt"
    set prompt to request.body["prompt"]
    if prompt is null:
        respond with {error: "prompt is required"}
    set plen to length prompt
    if plen is above max_prompt_length:
        respond with {error: "prompt exceeds max length"}
    set result to generate_full_app with prompt
    log "NOVA codegen: /generate completed"
    respond with result

to handle_generate_api:
    purpose: "Generate an API-type NC service from a prompt"
    set prompt to request.body["prompt"]
    set entities to request.body["entities"] or null
    if prompt is null:
        respond with {error: "prompt is required"}
    if entities is null:
        set analysis to analyze_prompt with prompt
        set entities to analysis["entities"]
    set svc_name to request.body["service_name"] or entities[0] + "-api"
    set svc_port to request.body["port"] or default_service_port
    set spec to {app_type: "api", entities: entities, service_name: svc_name, port: svc_port}
    set svc to generate_service with spec
    set eps to generate_endpoints with entities
    set models to []
    set default_fields to ["id", "name", "created_at", "updated_at"]
    repeat for each ent in entities:
        set ent_model to generate_model with ent, default_fields
        append ent_model to models
    respond with {service: svc, endpoints: eps, models: models}

to handle_list_examples:
    purpose: "List all available example NC applications"
    set listing to []
    repeat for each ex in examples:
        append {name: ex["name"], prompt: ex["prompt"]} to listing
    set ex_count to length examples
    respond with {count: ex_count, examples: listing}

to handle_get_example:
    purpose: "Return a specific example NC application by index"
    set idx to request.params.index
    set ex_count to length examples
    set idx_invalid to idx is below 0
    if idx_invalid is true:
        respond with {error: "invalid example index"}
    if idx is above ex_count:
        respond with {error: "invalid example index"}
    respond with examples[idx]

to health:
    purpose: "Health check for nova-codegen service"
    set ex_count to length examples
    respond with {service: "nova-codegen", status: "ok", version: "1.0.0", templates: 6, examples: ex_count, uptime: uptime()}

api:
    POST /generate runs handle_generate
    POST /generate/api runs handle_generate_api
    GET /examples runs handle_list_examples
    GET /examples/:index runs handle_get_example
    GET /health runs health

// === FILE: nc-ai/cortex/data.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NOVA Data Pipeline — Written in NC
//
//  Prepares training data for the NOVA model:
//    1. Load raw text from files
//    2. Clean and normalize
//    3. Extract triplets for graph building
//    4. Tokenize for SSM training
//    5. Generate template training pairs
//
//  Usage:
//    nc nc-ai/nova/data.nc
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service "nova-data"
version "1.0.0"

configure:
    corpus_dir is "./nc-ai/training_data/nc_corpus"
    output_dir is "./nc-ai/nova/data"
    min_sentence_length is 5
    max_sentence_length is 200

// ── Load All Corpus Files ─────────────────────────────────

to load_all_corpus:
    purpose: "Load all training corpus files"
    set files to []
    set total_chars to 0
    // NC corpus files (existing)
    set corpus_names to [
        "01_nc_engine_source.txt",
        "02_nc_language_spec.txt",
        "03_nc_stdlib.txt",
        "04_nc_examples.txt",
        "05_nc_tests.txt",
        "06_nc_ai_system.txt",
        "07_nc_ui_language.txt",
        "08_hiveant_system.txt",
        "09_swarmops_platform.txt",
        "10_neuraledge_finance.txt",
        "11_nc_docs.txt",
        "12_nc_apps.txt",
        "13_nc_scripts.txt",
        "14_website.txt"
    ]
    repeat for each name in corpus_names:
        set path to corpus_dir + "/" + name
        try:
            set content to read_file(path)
            if len(content) is above 0:
                append {"name": name, "content": content} to files
                set total_chars to total_chars + len(content)
                log "Loaded: " + name + " (" + str(len(content)) + " chars)"
        on error:
            log "Skipped: " + name
    log "Total: " + str(len(files)) + " files, " + str(total_chars) + " characters"
    respond with files

// ── Clean Text ────────────────────────────────────────────

to clean_text with text:
    purpose: "Clean and normalize text for training"
    set result to text
    // Remove excessive whitespace
    set result to replace(result, "\t", "    ")
    set result to replace(result, "\r", "")
    // Remove very long lines (likely minified/binary)
    set lines to split(result, "\n")
    set clean_lines to []
    repeat for each line in lines:
        if len(line) is below 500:
            append line to clean_lines
    set result to join(clean_lines, "\n")
    respond with result

// ── Extract Sentences ─────────────────────────────────────

to extract_sentences with text:
    purpose: "Split text into clean sentences"
    set raw_sentences to split(text, ".")
    set sentences to []
    repeat for each s in raw_sentences:
        set trimmed to trim(s)
        if len(trimmed) is above min_sentence_length:
            if len(trimmed) is below max_sentence_length:
                append trimmed to sentences
    respond with sentences

// ── Extract Triplets ──────────────────────────────────────

to extract_triplets with sentences:
    purpose: "Extract subject-relation-object triplets from sentences"
    set relation_words to ["is", "has", "gives", "causes", "contains", "makes", "leads", "produces", "creates", "uses", "needs", "runs", "provides", "supports", "enables", "requires", "defines", "stores", "handles", "implements", "extends", "includes", "generates", "processes", "manages", "controls", "monitors", "validates", "transforms", "connects"]
    set triplets to []
    repeat for each sentence in sentences:
        set words to split(sentence, " ")
        set i to 0
        repeat while i is below len(words) - 2:
            set mid to lower(trim(words[i + 1]))
            set is_rel to false
            repeat for each rw in relation_words:
                if mid is equal rw:
                    set is_rel to true
            if is_rel is equal true:
                set subject to lower(trim(words[i]))
                set object to lower(trim(words[i + 2]))
                if len(subject) is above 1:
                    if len(object) is above 1:
                        append {"subject": subject, "relation": mid, "object": object} to triplets
            set i to i + 1
    log "Extracted " + str(len(triplets)) + " triplets"
    respond with triplets

// ── Generate Training Pairs ───────────────────────────────

to generate_training_pairs with sentences:
    purpose: "Generate input-output pairs for template learning"
    set pairs to []
    repeat for each sentence in sentences:
        // Create Q&A style pairs
        set words to split(sentence, " ")
        if len(words) is above 3:
            // "What is X?" → sentence containing X
            set entity to words[0]
            set question to "what is " + entity
            append {"input": question, "output": sentence} to pairs
            // "Explain X" → sentence
            set explain to "explain " + entity
            append {"input": explain, "output": sentence} to pairs
    log "Generated " + str(len(pairs)) + " training pairs"
    respond with pairs

// ── Build Complete Dataset ────────────────────────────────

to build_dataset:
    purpose: "Build complete training dataset from corpus"
    log "╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
    log "║     NOVA Data Pipeline                         ║"
    log "╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
    // Load corpus
    set files to run load_all_corpus
    // Process each file
    set all_sentences to []
    set all_triplets to []
    set all_pairs to []
    set all_text to ""
    repeat for each file in files:
        set cleaned to run clean_text with file.content
        set sentences to run extract_sentences with cleaned
        set triplets to run extract_triplets with sentences
        set pairs to run generate_training_pairs with sentences
        repeat for each s in sentences:
            append s to all_sentences
        repeat for each t in triplets:
            append t to all_triplets
        repeat for each p in pairs:
            append p to all_pairs
        set all_text to all_text + cleaned + "\n"
    log "═══════════════════════════════════════════════"
    log "Dataset Summary:"
    log "  Files:      " + str(len(files))
    log "  Sentences:  " + str(len(all_sentences))
    log "  Triplets:   " + str(len(all_triplets))
    log "  QA Pairs:   " + str(len(all_pairs))
    log "  Total chars: " + str(len(all_text))
    log "═══════════════════════════════════════════════"
    respond with {
        "sentences": all_sentences,
        "triplets": all_triplets,
        "pairs": all_pairs,
        "raw_text": all_text,
        "stats": {
            "files": len(files),
            "sentences": len(all_sentences),
            "triplets": len(all_triplets),
            "pairs": len(all_pairs),
            "chars": len(all_text)
        }
    }

// ── Export Dataset ────────────────────────────────────────

to export_dataset with dataset:
    purpose: "Export processed dataset to files"
    // Export triplets
    set triplet_json to json_encode(dataset.triplets)
    store triplet_json to output_dir + "/triplets.json"
    log "Exported triplets to " + output_dir + "/triplets.json"
    // Export training pairs
    set pairs_json to json_encode(dataset.pairs)
    store pairs_json to output_dir + "/pairs.json"
    log "Exported pairs to " + output_dir + "/pairs.json"
    // Export raw text
    store dataset.raw_text to output_dir + "/corpus.txt"
    log "Exported corpus to " + output_dir + "/corpus.txt"
    respond with true

// ── API ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

api:
    POST /build runs build_dataset
    POST /export runs export_dataset
    GET /health runs health

to health:
    purpose: "Health check"
    respond with {"status": "ok", "service": "nova-data"}

// === FILE: nc-ai/cortex/deploy.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NOVA Deployment Orchestrator — Written in NC
//
//  Full lifecycle: Build → Test → Audit → Train → Benchmark →
//                  Sign → Deploy → Health Check
//
//  Deployment modes:
//    1. Local    — run directly on host machine
//    2. Docker   — containerized with resource limits
//    3. Native   — systemd (Linux) / launchd (macOS) service
//    4. Edge     — minimal binary for IoT / mobile devices
//
//  One command to go from source code to running NOVA model.
//
//  Usage:
//    nc nc-ai/cortex/deploy.nc
//    curl -X POST http://localhost:8700/deploy/full \
//      -d '{"model_size": "base", "mode": "docker"}'
//
//  Patent: DevHeal Labs AI — NOVA Model Architecture
//  Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI. All rights reserved.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service "nova-deploy"
version "1.0.0"

configure:
    port is 8700
    engine_dir is "./nc-engine"
    model_dir is "./nc-ai/nova/model"
    build_dir is "./build"
    artifact_dir is "./artifacts"
    docker_image is "nova-model"
    docker_tag is "latest"
    sign_key_path is "./keys/nova-sign.key"
    health_timeout is 30
    rollback_limit is 5

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  VERSION TRACKING
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to init:
    purpose: "Initialize deployment state, version history, model presets, and service start time"
    set deploy_state to {
        "current_version": "0.0.0",
        "previous_version": "0.0.0",
        "versions": [],
        "status": "idle",
        "last_deploy": 0,
        "last_error": "",
        "rollback_available": false
    }

    set version_history to []

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    //  MODEL SIZE PRESETS
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    set model_presets to {
        "micro": {
            "dim": 64,
            "state_dim": 8,
            "n_layers": 2,
            "vocab_size": 4096,
            "max_seq": 256,
            "ff_dim": 256,
            "graph_dim": 32,
            "n_templates": 16,
            "description": "Tiny model for testing and edge devices",
            "ram_mb": 50,
            "train_hours": 0.5
        },
        "small": {
            "dim": 128,
            "state_dim": 16,
            "n_layers": 4,
