// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  BUILD PIPELINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to build_engine:
    purpose: "Compile the NOVA C engine from source"
    log "═══ NOVA Build Pipeline ═══"
    log "Cleaning previous build artifacts..."

    set clean_result to run_command("make clean", engine_dir)
    if clean_result.exit_code is not 0:
        log "Warning: clean had issues, proceeding anyway"

    log "Compiling NOVA C engine..."
    set build_result to run_command("make", engine_dir)

    if build_result.exit_code is not 0:
        set deploy_state.last_error to build_result.stderr
        log "BUILD FAILED: " + build_result.stderr
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "build", "error": build_result.stderr}

    log "Build complete. Binary size: " + get_file_size(build_dir + "/nova")
    respond with {"success": true, "stage": "build", "binary": build_dir + "/nova"}

to run_unit_tests:
    purpose: "Execute the full NOVA test suite"
    log "═══ Running Unit Tests ═══"

    set test_result to run_command("make test", engine_dir)

    if test_result.exit_code is not 0:
        log "TESTS FAILED: " + test_result.stderr
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "test", "error": test_result.stderr}

    set test_output to parse_test_results(test_result.stdout)
    log "Tests passed: " + test_output.passed + "/" + test_output.total
    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "stage": "test",
        "passed": test_output.passed,
        "failed": test_output.failed,
        "total": test_output.total
    }

to run_security_audit:
    purpose: "Run security checks on the compiled binary"
    log "═══ Security Audit ═══"

    set checks to [
        "buffer_overflow_scan",
        "memory_leak_check",
        "dependency_audit",
        "symbol_validation",
        "stack_protection_verify"
    ]

    set results to []
    repeat for each check in checks:
        log "Running: " + check
        set result to run_security_check(check, build_dir + "/nova")
        append result to results

        if result.severity is "critical":
            log "CRITICAL: " + check + " — " + result.message
            respond with {"success": false, "stage": "audit", "critical": check, "details": result}

    set passed to count_where(results, "status", "pass")
    log "Security audit: " + passed + "/" + length(results) + " checks passed"
    respond with {"success": true, "stage": "audit", "checks": results}

to run_benchmarks:
    purpose: "Benchmark NOVA inference speed, memory, and throughput"
    log "═══ Running Benchmarks ═══"

    set bench_config to {
        "iterations": 1000,
        "warmup": 100,
        "prompt_lengths": [32, 128, 512, 1024],
        "batch_sizes": [1, 4, 8]
    }

    set bench_result to run_command("make benchmark", engine_dir)

    if bench_result.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "benchmark", "error": bench_result.stderr}

    set metrics to parse_benchmark_output(bench_result.stdout)
    log "Latency p50: " + metrics.p50_ms + "ms | p99: " + metrics.p99_ms + "ms"
    log "Throughput: " + metrics.tokens_per_sec + " tokens/sec"
    log "Peak memory: " + metrics.peak_memory_mb + " MB"

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "stage": "benchmark",
        "latency_p50_ms": metrics.p50_ms,
        "latency_p99_ms": metrics.p99_ms,
        "tokens_per_sec": metrics.tokens_per_sec,
        "peak_memory_mb": metrics.peak_memory_mb
    }

to sign_binary with binary_path:
    purpose: "Cryptographically sign the NOVA binary for integrity verification"
    log "═══ Signing Binary ═══"

    if not file_exists(sign_key_path):
        log "Generating new signing key..."
        set keygen_result to run_command("openssl genpkey -algorithm ed25519 -out " + sign_key_path)
        if keygen_result.exit_code is not 0:
            respond with {"success": false, "stage": "sign", "error": "Key generation failed"}

    set hash to compute_sha256(binary_path)
    log "Binary SHA-256: " + hash

    set sig_path to binary_path + ".sig"
    set sign_result to run_command("openssl pkeyutl -sign -inkey " + sign_key_path + " -in " + binary_path + " -out " + sig_path)

    if sign_result.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "sign", "error": sign_result.stderr}

    log "Signed: " + sig_path
    respond with {"success": true, "stage": "sign", "signature": sig_path, "sha256": hash}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  TRAINING PIPELINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to configure_model with size_name:
    purpose: "Load model configuration for the given size preset"

    if size_name is not in model_presets:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Unknown model size: " + size_name + ". Use: micro, small, base, large, 1b, 7b, 20b"}

    set config to model_presets[size_name]
    log "Model preset: " + size_name + " — " + config.description
    log "Estimated RAM: " + config.ram_mb + " MB | Training time: ~" + config.train_hours + " hours"
    respond with {"success": true, "config": config, "size": size_name}

to run_training with model_size, data_path:
    purpose: "Execute the full 3-phase NOVA training pipeline"
    log "═══ NOVA Training Pipeline ═══"
    log "Model size: " + model_size

    set config_result to configure_model(model_size)
    if config_result.success is false:
        respond with config_result

    set config to config_result.config

    // Phase 1: Neural SSM Training
    log "── Phase 1: Neural SSM Training ──"
    set phase1 to run_command("nc nc-ai/cortex/train.nc --phase 1 --config '" + to_json(config) + "' --data " + data_path)
    if phase1.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "train", "phase": 1, "error": phase1.stderr}
    log "Phase 1 complete. Loss: " + parse_loss(phase1.stdout)

    // Phase 2: Knowledge Graph Building
    log "── Phase 2: Knowledge Graph Building ──"
    set phase2 to run_command("nc nc-ai/cortex/train.nc --phase 2 --config '" + to_json(config) + "' --data " + data_path)
    if phase2.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "train", "phase": 2, "error": phase2.stderr}
    log "Phase 2 complete. Graph nodes: " + parse_graph_nodes(phase2.stdout)

    // Phase 3: Template + Hebbian Learning
    log "── Phase 3: Template + Hebbian Learning ──"
    set phase3 to run_command("nc nc-ai/cortex/train.nc --phase 3 --config '" + to_json(config) + "' --data " + data_path)
    if phase3.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "train", "phase": 3, "error": phase3.stderr}
    log "Phase 3 complete. Templates learned: " + parse_templates(phase3.stdout)

    log "All 3 training phases complete."
    respond with {"success": true, "stage": "train", "model_size": model_size}

to validate_model with model_path:
    purpose: "Validate a trained NOVA model before deployment"
    log "═══ Validating Trained Model ═══"

    set checks to {
        "file_exists": file_exists(model_path),
        "file_size": get_file_size(model_path),
        "magic_bytes": check_magic_bytes(model_path, "NOVA"),
        "checksum_valid": verify_checksum(model_path)
    }

    if checks.file_exists is false:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "validate", "error": "Model file not found: " + model_path}

    if checks.magic_bytes is false:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "validate", "error": "Invalid model format — missing NOVA header"}

    // Quick inference test
    set test_prompt to "What is NOVA?"
    set inference_result to run_command("nc nc-ai/cortex/inference.nc --model " + model_path + " --prompt '" + test_prompt + "' --max-tokens 32")

    if inference_result.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "validate", "error": "Inference test failed"}

    log "Model validation passed. Size: " + checks.file_size + " bytes"
    respond with {"success": true, "stage": "validate", "model": model_path, "size": checks.file_size}

to export_artifacts with model_size:
    purpose: "Export trained model and metadata to artifact directory"
    log "═══ Exporting Artifacts ═══"

    set deploy_version to generate_version()
    set artifact_path to artifact_dir + "/nova-" + model_size + "-v" + deploy_version

    create_directory(artifact_path)

    // Copy model files
    copy_file(model_dir + "/nova_final.bin", artifact_path + "/nova_final.bin")
    copy_file(model_dir + "/nova_graph.bin", artifact_path + "/nova_graph.bin")
    copy_file(model_dir + "/nova_vocab.json", artifact_path + "/nova_vocab.json")

    // Write metadata
    set metadata to {
        "version": deploy_version,
        "model_size": model_size,
        "config": model_presets[model_size],
        "exported_at": current_timestamp(),
        "engine_version": "1.0.0",
        "patent": "DevHeal Labs AI — NOVA Model Architecture",
        "copyright": "2026 DevHeal Labs AI"
    }
    write_file(artifact_path + "/metadata.json", to_json(metadata))

    log "Artifacts exported to: " + artifact_path
    respond with {"success": true, "stage": "export", "path": artifact_path, "version": deploy_version}

to sign_model with artifact_path:
    purpose: "Sign all model files in the artifact directory"
    log "═══ Signing Model Files ═══"

    set files to list_files(artifact_path)
    set signed_count to 0

    repeat for each file in files:
        if ends_with(file, ".bin") or ends_with(file, ".json"):
            set sig_result to sign_binary(artifact_path + "/" + file)
            if sig_result.success is false:
                respond with {"success": false, "stage": "sign_model", "file": file, "error": sig_result.error}
            set signed_count to signed_count + 1
            log "Signed: " + file

    log "Signed " + signed_count + " model files"
    respond with {"success": true, "stage": "sign_model", "files_signed": signed_count}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  DEPLOYMENT MODES
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to deploy_local with artifact_path:
    purpose: "Deploy NOVA directly on the host machine"
    log "═══ Local Deployment ═══"

    set binary to build_dir + "/nova"
    if not file_exists(binary):
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "deploy_local", "error": "Binary not found. Run build first."}

    set model_file to artifact_path + "/nova_final.bin"
    if not file_exists(model_file):
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "deploy_local", "error": "Model not found at: " + model_file}

    log "Starting NOVA inference server locally..."
    set run_result to run_command(binary + " serve --model " + model_file + " --port 8300 --daemon")

    if run_result.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "deploy_local", "error": run_result.stderr}

    set pid to parse_pid(run_result.stdout)
    log "NOVA running locally. PID: " + pid + " | Port: 8300"
    respond with {"success": true, "stage": "deploy_local", "pid": pid, "port": 8300}

to deploy_docker with artifact_path, resource_limits:
    purpose: "Deploy NOVA in a Docker container with resource controls"
    log "═══ Docker Deployment ═══"

    // Generate Dockerfile
    set dockerfile to generate_dockerfile(artifact_path)
    write_file(artifact_path + "/Dockerfile", dockerfile)
    log "Dockerfile generated"

    // Build image
    log "Building Docker image: " + docker_image + ":" + docker_tag
    set build_cmd to "docker build -t " + docker_image + ":" + docker_tag + " " + artifact_path
    set build_result to run_command(build_cmd)

    if build_result.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "deploy_docker", "error": build_result.stderr}

    // Run container
    set mem_limit to resource_limits.memory or "2g"
    set cpu_limit to resource_limits.cpus or "2"
    set run_cmd to "docker run -d --name nova-server"
    set run_cmd to run_cmd + " --memory=" + mem_limit
    set run_cmd to run_cmd + " --cpus=" + cpu_limit
    set run_cmd to run_cmd + " -p 8300:8300"
    set run_cmd to run_cmd + " --restart=unless-stopped"
    set run_cmd to run_cmd + " " + docker_image + ":" + docker_tag

    log "Running: " + run_cmd
    set run_result to run_command(run_cmd)

    if run_result.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "deploy_docker", "error": run_result.stderr}

    set container_id to trim(run_result.stdout)
    log "Container started: " + container_id
    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "stage": "deploy_docker",
        "container_id": container_id,
        "image": docker_image + ":" + docker_tag,
        "port": 8300,
        "memory": mem_limit,
        "cpus": cpu_limit
    }

to deploy_native_service with artifact_path:
    purpose: "Install NOVA as a native system service (systemd or launchd)"
    log "═══ Native Service Deployment ═══"

    set platform to detect_platform()

    if platform is "linux":
        set service_file to generate_systemd_unit(artifact_path)
        write_file("/etc/systemd/system/nova.service", service_file)
        run_command("systemctl daemon-reload")
        run_command("systemctl enable nova")
        run_command("systemctl start nova")
        log "Installed systemd service: nova.service"
        respond with {"success": true, "stage": "deploy_native", "platform": "linux", "service": "nova.service"}

    if platform is "macos":
        set plist to generate_launchd_plist(artifact_path)
        set plist_path to "/Library/LaunchDaemons/ai.devheal.nova.plist"
        write_file(plist_path, plist)
        run_command("launchctl load " + plist_path)
        log "Installed launchd service: ai.devheal.nova"
        respond with {"success": true, "stage": "deploy_native", "platform": "macos", "service": "ai.devheal.nova"}

    respond with {"success": false, "stage": "deploy_native", "error": "Unsupported platform: " + platform}

to deploy_edge with artifact_path, target:
    purpose: "Build and deploy minimal NOVA binary for edge/IoT/mobile devices"
    log "═══ Edge Deployment ═══"
    log "Target: " + target

    set supported_targets to ["arm64", "armv7", "riscv64", "wasm", "x86_embedded"]

    if target is not in supported_targets:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "deploy_edge", "error": "Unsupported target: " + target + ". Supported: " + join(supported_targets, ", ")}

    // Cross-compile minimal binary
    log "Cross-compiling for " + target + "..."
    set cross_cmd to "make edge TARGET=" + target + " MODEL_SIZE=micro STRIP=1 LTO=1"
    set cross_result to run_command(cross_cmd, engine_dir)

    if cross_result.exit_code is not 0:
        respond with {"success": false, "stage": "deploy_edge", "error": cross_result.stderr}

    set edge_binary to build_dir + "/nova-edge-" + target
    set binary_size to get_file_size(edge_binary)
    log "Edge binary: " + edge_binary + " (" + format_size(binary_size) + ")"

    // Package with micro model
    set edge_pkg to artifact_path + "/nova-edge-" + target + ".tar.gz"
    set pack_cmd to "tar czf " + edge_pkg + " -C " + build_dir + " nova-edge-" + target + " -C " + artifact_path + " nova_final.bin"
    run_command(pack_cmd)

    log "Edge package: " + edge_pkg
    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "stage": "deploy_edge",
        "target": target,
        "binary": edge_binary,
        "binary_size": binary_size,
        "package": edge_pkg
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  DOCKER SUPPORT
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to generate_dockerfile with artifact_path:
    purpose: "Generate a multi-stage Alpine-based Dockerfile for NOVA"

    set dockerfile to "# NOVA — Neural Optimized Vector Architecture\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "# Multi-stage Docker build\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "# Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI. All rights reserved.\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "# Stage 1: Build the C engine\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "FROM alpine:3.19 AS builder\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "RUN apk add --no-cache gcc musl-dev make openssl-dev\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "WORKDIR /nova\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "COPY nc-engine/ ./nc-engine/\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "COPY Makefile .\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "RUN make clean && make STATIC=1 LTO=1\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "# Stage 2: Minimal runtime image\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "FROM alpine:3.19 AS runtime\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "RUN apk add --no-cache libssl3 ca-certificates\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "WORKDIR /nova\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "COPY --from=builder /nova/build/nova /usr/local/bin/nova\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "COPY " + artifact_path + "/nova_final.bin ./model/nova_final.bin\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "COPY " + artifact_path + "/nova_graph.bin ./model/nova_graph.bin\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "COPY " + artifact_path + "/nova_vocab.json ./model/nova_vocab.json\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "COPY " + artifact_path + "/metadata.json ./model/metadata.json\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "RUN chown -R nova:nova /nova\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "USER nova\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "EXPOSE 8300\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=5s --retries=3 CMD wget -qO- http://localhost:8300/health\n\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "ENTRYPOINT [\"nova\", \"serve\"]\n"
    set dockerfile to dockerfile + "CMD [\"--model\", \"./model/nova_final.bin\", \"--port\", \"8300\"]\n"

    respond with dockerfile

to generate_systemd_unit with artifact_path:
    purpose: "Generate a systemd service unit file"

    set unit to "[Unit]\n"
    set unit to unit + "Description=NOVA — Neural Optimized Vector Architecture\n"
    set unit to unit + "After=network.target\n"
    set unit to unit + "Documentation=https://devheal.ai/nova\n\n"
    set unit to unit + "[Service]\n"
    set unit to unit + "Type=simple\n"
    set unit to unit + "User=nova\n"
    set unit to unit + "Group=nova\n"
    set unit to unit + "ExecStart=/usr/local/bin/nova serve --model " + artifact_path + "/nova_final.bin --port 8300\n"
    set unit to unit + "Restart=on-failure\n"
    set unit to unit + "RestartSec=5\n"
    set unit to unit + "LimitNOFILE=65535\n"
    set unit to unit + "MemoryMax=2G\n"
    set unit to unit + "CPUQuota=200%\n\n"
    set unit to unit + "[Install]\n"
    set unit to unit + "WantedBy=multi-user.target\n"

    respond with unit

to generate_launchd_plist with artifact_path:
    purpose: "Generate a macOS launchd plist file"

    set plist to "<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>\n"
    set plist to plist + "<!DOCTYPE plist PUBLIC \"-//Apple//DTD PLIST 1.0//EN\" \"http://www.apple.com/DTDs/PropertyList-1.0.dtd\">\n"
    set plist to plist + "<plist version=\"1.0\">\n"
    set plist to plist + "<dict>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <key>Label</key>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <string>ai.devheal.nova</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <key>ProgramArguments</key>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <array>\n"
    set plist to plist + "        <string>/usr/local/bin/nova</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "        <string>serve</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "        <string>--model</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "        <string>" + artifact_path + "/nova_final.bin</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "        <string>--port</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "        <string>8300</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    </array>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <key>RunAtLoad</key>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <true/>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <key>KeepAlive</key>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <true/>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <key>StandardOutPath</key>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <string>/var/log/nova/nova.log</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <key>StandardErrorPath</key>\n"
    set plist to plist + "    <string>/var/log/nova/nova-error.log</string>\n"
    set plist to plist + "</dict>\n"
    set plist to plist + "</plist>\n"

    respond with plist

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HEALTH CHECK & ROLLBACK
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to check_health with host, port:
    purpose: "Verify the deployed NOVA service is healthy"
    log "═══ Health Check ═══"

    set url to "http://" + host + ":" + to_str(port) + "/health"
    set attempts to 0
    set max_attempts to health_timeout

    set healthy to false
    set health_body to {}
    set health_response to poll_health(url, max_attempts)
    set healthy to health_response.healthy
    set health_body to health_response.body
    if healthy is true:
        respond with {
            "success": true,
            "healthy": true,
            "uptime": health_body.uptime,
            "model_loaded": health_body.model_loaded,
            "inference_ready": health_body.inference_ready
        }
    log "Health check FAILED after " + max_attempts + " attempts"
    respond with {"success": false, "healthy": false, "error": "Service did not become healthy within " + max_attempts + "s"}

to poll_health with url, max_attempts:
    purpose: "Poll the health endpoint until it responds or timeout"
    set attempts to 0
    repeat while attempts is below max_attempts:
        set response to http_get(url)
        set attempts to attempts + 1
        wait(1000)
    set last_response to http_get(url)
    if last_response.status is 200:
        respond with {"healthy": true, "body": parse_json(last_response.body)}
    respond with {"healthy": false, "body": {}}


to rollback:
    purpose: "Rollback to the previous deployed version"
    log "═══ Rollback ═══"

    if deploy_state.rollback_available is false:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "No previous version available for rollback"}

    set prev_version to deploy_state.previous_version
    log "Rolling back from " + deploy_state.current_version + " to " + prev_version

    set prev_artifact to artifact_dir + "/nova-v" + prev_version

    if not file_exists(prev_artifact):
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Previous artifact not found: " + prev_artifact}

    // Stop current deployment
    log "Stopping current deployment..."
    try:
        run_command("docker stop nova-server && docker rm nova-server")
    on error:
        try:
            run_command("systemctl stop nova")
        on error:
            run_command("pkill -f 'nova serve'")

    // Deploy previous version
    log "Deploying previous version: " + prev_version
    set result to deploy_local(prev_artifact)

    if result.success is true:
        set deploy_state.current_version to prev_version
        set deploy_state.rollback_available to false
        set deploy_state.status to "rolled_back"
        log "Rollback successful. Running version: " + prev_version

    respond with result

to track_version with ver, artifact_path, mode:
    purpose: "Record a deployment version in the history"

    set entry to {
        "version": ver,
        "artifact_path": artifact_path,
        "mode": mode,
        "deployed_at": current_timestamp(),
        "status": "active"
    }

    // Mark previous entries as inactive
    repeat for each v in version_history:
        set v.status to "inactive"

    append entry to version_history

    set deploy_state.previous_version to deploy_state.current_version
    set deploy_state.current_version to ver
    set deploy_state.rollback_available to true
    set deploy_state.last_deploy to current_timestamp()

    // Enforce rollback limit
    if length(version_history) is above rollback_limit:
        set oldest to version_history[0]
        log "Pruning old version: " + oldest.version
        delete_directory(oldest.artifact_path)
        remove_first(version_history)

    respond with entry

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  FULL DEPLOY COMMAND
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to full_deploy with model_size, deploy_mode, data_path, resource_limits:
    purpose: "Complete pipeline: Build → Test → Audit → Train → Benchmark → Sign → Deploy"
    log "╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
    log "║      NOVA — Full Deployment Pipeline                     ║"
    log "║      Neural Optimized Vector Architecture                ║"
    log "║      Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI                      ║"
    log "╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
    log ""
    log "Model size: " + model_size
    log "Deploy mode: " + deploy_mode
    log "Data path: " + data_path

    set deploy_state.status to "running"
    set start_time to current_timestamp()

    // Step 1: Build
    log ""
    log "[1/7] Building C engine..."
    set build_result to build_engine()
    if build_result.success is false:
        set deploy_state.status to "failed"
        respond with {"success": false, "failed_at": "build", "error": build_result.error}

    // Step 2: Test
    log ""
    log "[2/7] Running unit tests..."
    set test_result to run_unit_tests()
    if test_result.success is false:
        set deploy_state.status to "failed"
        respond with {"success": false, "failed_at": "test", "error": test_result.error}

    // Step 3: Security audit
    log ""
    log "[3/7] Running security audit..."
    set audit_result to run_security_audit()
    if audit_result.success is false:
        set deploy_state.status to "failed"
        respond with {"success": false, "failed_at": "audit", "error": audit_result.error}

    // Step 4: Train
    log ""
    log "[4/7] Training NOVA model (" + model_size + ")..."
    set train_result to run_training(model_size, data_path)
    if train_result.success is false:
        set deploy_state.status to "failed"
        respond with {"success": false, "failed_at": "train", "error": train_result.error}

    // Step 5: Benchmark
    log ""
    log "[5/7] Running benchmarks..."
    set bench_result to run_benchmarks()
    if bench_result.success is false:
        log "Warning: Benchmarks failed, continuing deployment"

    // Step 6: Sign
    log ""
    log "[6/7] Signing binary and model..."
    set sign_bin to sign_binary(build_dir + "/nova")
    set export_result to export_artifacts(model_size)
    set sign_model_result to sign_model(export_result.path)

    // Step 7: Deploy
    log ""
    log "[7/7] Deploying (" + deploy_mode + ")..."

    set deploy_result to {}

    if deploy_mode is "local":
        set deploy_result to deploy_local(export_result.path)

    if deploy_mode is "docker":
        set deploy_result to deploy_docker(export_result.path, resource_limits)

    if deploy_mode is "native":
        set deploy_result to deploy_native_service(export_result.path)

    if deploy_mode is "edge":
        set target to resource_limits.target or "arm64"
        set deploy_result to deploy_edge(export_result.path, target)

    if deploy_result.success is false:
        set deploy_state.status to "failed"
        respond with {"success": false, "failed_at": "deploy", "error": deploy_result.error}

    // Post-deploy health check
    log ""
    log "Running post-deployment health check..."
    set health to check_health("localhost", 8300)

    if health.success is false:
        log "Health check failed. Initiating rollback..."
        set rollback_result to rollback()
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "failed_at": "health_check",
            "rollback": rollback_result.success,
            "error": "Deployment unhealthy, rolled back"
        }

    // Track version
    track_version(export_result.version, export_result.path, deploy_mode)
    set deploy_state.status to "deployed"

    set elapsed to current_timestamp() - start_time
    log ""
    log "╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
    log "║      NOVA Deployment Complete                            ║"
    log "║      Version: " + export_result.version + "                            ║"
    log "║      Mode: " + deploy_mode + "                                    ║"
    log "║      Time: " + format_duration(elapsed) + "                          ║"
    log "╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "version": export_result.version,
        "mode": deploy_mode,
        "model_size": model_size,
        "elapsed_seconds": elapsed,
        "benchmark": bench_result,
        "health": health
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  API ENDPOINTS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

api:
    POST /deploy/full runs api_deploy_full
    POST /deploy/build runs api_deploy_build
    POST /deploy/train runs api_deploy_train
    POST /deploy/docker runs api_deploy_docker
    POST /deploy/sign runs api_deploy_sign
    POST /rollback runs api_rollback
    GET /versions runs api_get_versions
    GET /health runs api_health

to api_deploy_full:
    purpose: "Full pipeline: source → running NOVA model"

    set body to request.body
    set model_size to body.model_size or "base"
    set deploy_mode to body.mode or "local"
    set data_path to body.data_path or "./nc-ai/training_data"
    set resource_limits to body.resource_limits or {"memory": "2g", "cpus": "2"}

    set result_data to full_deploy(model_size, deploy_mode, data_path, resource_limits)
    respond with result_data

to api_deploy_build:
    purpose: "Build the C engine only"

    set build_result to build_engine()
    if build_result.success is false:
        respond with build_result

    set test_result to run_unit_tests()
    respond with {
        "build": build_result,
        "tests": test_result
    }

to api_deploy_train:
    purpose: "Train a NOVA model"

    set body to request.body
    set model_size to body.model_size or "base"
    set data_path to body.data_path or "./nc-ai/training_data"

    set train_result to run_training(model_size, data_path)

    if train_result.success is true:
        set validate_result to validate_model(model_dir + "/nova_final.bin")
        set export_result to export_artifacts(model_size)
        respond with {
            "train": train_result,
            "validation": validate_result,
            "artifacts": export_result
        }

    respond with train_result

to api_deploy_docker:
    purpose: "Build and run NOVA in Docker"

    set body to request.body
    set artifact_path to body.artifact_path or artifact_dir + "/latest"
    set resource_limits to body.resource_limits or {"memory": "2g", "cpus": "2"}

    set result_data to deploy_docker(artifact_path, resource_limits)
    respond with result_data

to api_deploy_sign:
    purpose: "Sign binary and model files"

    set body to request.body
    set binary_path to body.binary_path or build_dir + "/nova"
    set artifact_path to body.artifact_path or artifact_dir + "/latest"

    set bin_sig to sign_binary(binary_path)
    set model_sig to sign_model(artifact_path)

    respond with {
        "binary": bin_sig,
        "model": model_sig
    }

to api_rollback:
    purpose: "Rollback to the previous deployed version"

    set result_data to rollback()
    respond with result_data

to api_get_versions:
    purpose: "List all deployed versions"

    respond with {
        "current": deploy_state.current_version,
        "previous": deploy_state.previous_version,
        "history": version_history,
        "rollback_available": deploy_state.rollback_available
    }

to api_health:
    purpose: "Deployment orchestrator health status"

    respond with {
        "service": "nova-deploy",
        "status": "running",
        "deploy_state": deploy_state.status,
        "current_version": deploy_state.current_version,
        "last_deploy": deploy_state.last_deploy,
        "uptime": current_timestamp() - service_start_time
    }

// === FILE: nc-ai/cortex/enterprise.nc ===

//  NOVA Enterprise Edition — Written in NC

//    4. Audit Logging          — full event trail with retention

//      -d '{"name": "Acme Corp", "license_key": "NOVA-ENT-..."}'

//  Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI. All rights reserved.

service "nova-enterprise"

    port is 9000
    model_dir is "./nc-ai/cortex/model"
    data_dir is "./nc-ai/enterprise/data"
    audit_dir is "./nc-ai/enterprise/audit"

    heartbeat_interval is 10
    max_queue_size is 10000
    circuit_breaker_threshold is 5
    circuit_breaker_reset is 60
    default_retention_days is 90

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

//  License Key Format: NOVA-{TIER}-{ORG_HASH}-{EXPIRY}-{SIGNATURE}

//
//  Tiers:

//    Unlimited    — $999/mo, no limits
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
