// ── License Validation ────────────────────────────────────────────

to validate_license with key:
    purpose: "Validate a NOVA license key for format, expiry, and tier"
    log "Validating license key: " + mask_key(key)

    // Check format: NOVA-{TIER}-{ORG_HASH}-{EXPIRY}-{SIGNATURE}
    set parts to split(key, "-")
    if len(parts) is not 5:
        log "License validation FAILED: invalid format"
        respond with {
            "valid": false,
            "error": "Invalid license key format. Expected: NOVA-{TIER}-{ORG_HASH}-{EXPIRY}-{SIGNATURE}"
        }

    set prefix to parts[0]
    set tier_code to lower(parts[1])
    set org_hash to parts[2]
    set expiry_str to parts[3]
    set signature to parts[4]

    // Verify prefix
    if prefix is not "NOVA":
        respond with {"valid": false, "error": "Invalid license prefix"}

    // Map tier codes to tier names
    set tier_map to {
        "com": "community",
        "pro": "professional",
        "ent": "enterprise",
        "unl": "unlimited"
    }

    if tier_map[tier_code] is empty:
        respond with {"valid": false, "error": "Unknown license tier: " + tier_code}

    set tier_name to tier_map[tier_code]

    // Verify signature
    set expected_sig to hash(prefix + tier_code + org_hash + expiry_str + license_secret)
    set sig_prefix to substr(expected_sig, 0, 8)
    if signature is not sig_prefix:
        log "License validation FAILED: invalid signature"
        respond with {"valid": false, "error": "Invalid license signature"}

    // Check expiry
    set expiry_date to parse_date(expiry_str, "YYYYMMDD")
    set now to current_timestamp()
    if now is above expiry_date:
        log "License validation FAILED: expired on " + expiry_str
        respond with {
            "valid": false,
            "error": "License expired on " + expiry_str,
            "expired": true,
            "tier": tier_name
        }

    set tier_config to license_tiers[tier_name]
    log "License VALID: tier=" + tier_name + " org=" + org_hash + " expires=" + expiry_str

    respond with {
        "valid": true,
        "tier": tier_name,
        "tier_config": tier_config,
        "org_hash": org_hash,
        "expires": expiry_str,
        "days_remaining": days_between(now, expiry_date)
    }

// ── License Generation ────────────────────────────────────────────

to generate_license with tier, org, duration:
    purpose: "Generate a signed NOVA license key for an organization"
    log "Generating license: tier=" + tier + " org=" + org + " duration=" + duration + " months"

    // Validate tier
    if license_tiers[tier] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Unknown tier: " + tier}

    // Map tier to code
    set code_map to {
        "community": "COM",
        "professional": "PRO",
        "enterprise": "ENT",
        "unlimited": "UNL"
    }

    set tier_code to code_map[tier]
    set org_hash to substr(hash(org + current_timestamp()), 0, 8)
    set expiry_date to add_months(current_timestamp(), duration)
    set expiry_str to format_date(expiry_date, "YYYYMMDD")

    // Generate signature
    set raw_sig to hash("NOVA" + tier_code + org_hash + expiry_str + license_secret)
    set signature to substr(raw_sig, 0, 8)

    set license_key to "NOVA-" + tier_code + "-" + org_hash + "-" + expiry_str + "-" + signature

    // Store active license
    set active_licenses[license_key] to {
        "tier": tier,
        "org": org,
        "org_hash": org_hash,
        "created_at": current_timestamp(),
        "expires_at": expiry_date,
        "status": "active"
    }

    log "License generated: " + mask_key(license_key)

    set log_event to {
        "type": "license_generated",
        "tier": tier,
        "org": org,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "license_key": license_key,
        "tier": tier,
        "org": org,
        "expires": expiry_str,
        "tier_config": license_tiers[tier]
    }

// ── Feature Access Check ──────────────────────────────────────────

to check_feature with feature, license:
    purpose: "Verify whether a license tier has access to a specific feature"
    set validation to validate_license(license)
    if validation.valid is false:
        respond with {"allowed": false, "error": validation.error}

    set tier_config to validation.tier_config
    set features to tier_config.features_enabled

    repeat for each f in features:
        if f is feature:
            respond with {
                "allowed": true,
                "feature": feature,
                "tier": validation.tier
            }

    respond with {
        "allowed": false,
        "feature": feature,
        "tier": validation.tier,
        "error": "Feature '" + feature + "' not available in " + validation.tier + " tier"
    }

// ── Key Masking Utility ───────────────────────────────────────────

to mask_key with key:
    purpose: "Mask a license key for safe logging"
    if len(key) is below 12:
        respond with "****"
    set prefix to substr(key, 0, 9)
    set suffix to substr(key, len(key) - 4, len(key))
    respond with prefix + "****" + suffix

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECTION 2: MULTI-TENANT SaaS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
//  Each tenant gets:
//    - Isolated model instances
//    - Separate knowledge graphs
//    - Independent usage counters
//    - Per-tenant rate limiting
//    - Dedicated analytics
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to init_tenants:
    purpose: "Initialize multi-tenant state"
    set tenants to {}
    set tenant_counter to 0

// ── Tenant Provisioning ───────────────────────────────────────────

to create_tenant with name, license_key:
    purpose: "Provision a new isolated tenant with validated license"
    log "Creating tenant: " + name

    // Validate the license first
    set license_info to validate_license(license_key)
    if license_info.valid is false:
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "error": "Invalid license: " + license_info.error
        }

    // Generate tenant ID
    set tenant_counter to tenant_counter + 1
    set tenant_id to "tenant_" + hash(name + current_timestamp())
    set tenant_id to substr(tenant_id, 0, 16)

    // Build tenant config
    set tier_config to license_info.tier_config
    set tenant to {
        "id": tenant_id,
        "name": name,
        "license_key": license_key,
        "tier": license_info.tier,
        "created_at": current_timestamp(),
        "status": "active",
        "config": {
            "max_models": tier_config.max_models,
            "max_requests_per_min": tier_config.max_requests_per_min,
            "max_model_size": tier_config.max_model_size,
            "max_users": tier_config.max_users,
            "features_enabled": tier_config.features_enabled
        },
        "usage": {
            "total_requests": 0,
            "total_tokens": 0,
            "total_compute_ms": 0,
            "total_storage_bytes": 0,
            "requests_this_minute": 0,
            "minute_window_start": current_timestamp(),
            "errors": 0
        },
        "analytics": {
            "avg_latency_ms": 0,
            "p95_latency_ms": 0,
            "p99_latency_ms": 0,
            "latency_samples": [],
            "error_rate": 0,
            "last_request_at": 0
        },
        "models": [],
        "users": [],
        "api_keys": []
    }

    // Store tenant
    set tenants[tenant_id] to tenant

    // Create tenant data directories
    store {} to data_dir + "/tenants/" + tenant_id + "/config.json"
    store {} to data_dir + "/tenants/" + tenant_id + "/graph.json"

    // Audit the creation
    set log_event to {
        "type": "tenant_created",
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "tenant_name": name,
        "tier": license_info.tier,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    log "Tenant created: " + tenant_id + " (" + name + ") tier=" + license_info.tier

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "name": name,
        "tier": license_info.tier,
        "config": tenant.config
    }

// ── Tenant Retrieval ──────────────────────────────────────────────

to get_tenant with tenant_id:
    purpose: "Retrieve a tenant's full configuration and status"
    if tenants[tenant_id] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Tenant not found: " + tenant_id}

    set tenant to tenants[tenant_id]
    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "tenant": tenant
    }

// ── Tenant Inference Request ──────────────────────────────────────

to tenant_request with tenant_id, prompt:
    purpose: "Process an inference request with tenant isolation and rate limiting"
    set start_time to current_timestamp()

    // Verify tenant exists
    if tenants[tenant_id] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Tenant not found: " + tenant_id}

    set tenant to tenants[tenant_id]

    // Check tenant is active
    if tenant.status is not "active":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Tenant is " + tenant.status}

    // Rate limit check
    set now to current_timestamp()
    set t_usage to tenant.usage
    set t_config to tenant.config
    set t_analytics to tenant.analytics
    set window_elapsed to now - t_usage.minute_window_start
    if window_elapsed is above 60000:
        // Reset the minute window
        set t_usage.requests_this_minute to 0
        set t_usage.minute_window_start to now

    if t_usage.requests_this_minute is above t_config.max_requests_per_min:
        log "Rate limit exceeded for tenant " + tenant_id
        set log_event to {
            "type": "rate_limit_exceeded",
            "tenant_id": tenant_id,
            "timestamp": now
        }
        set _ to audit_log(log_event)
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "error": "Rate limit exceeded. Max " + t_config.max_requests_per_min + " requests/min for " + tenant.tier + " tier"
        }

    // Increment usage counters
    set t_usage.requests_this_minute to t_usage.requests_this_minute + 1
    set t_usage.total_requests to t_usage.total_requests + 1

    // Process inference through NOVA engine
    try:
        set result to nova_infer(prompt, tenant_id)
        set elapsed to current_timestamp() - start_time

        // Update analytics
        set t_usage.total_tokens to t_usage.total_tokens + result.tokens_used
        set t_usage.total_compute_ms to t_usage.total_compute_ms + elapsed
        set t_analytics.last_request_at to now
        append elapsed to t_analytics.latency_samples

        // Recalculate average latency
        set total_latency to 0
        set sample_count to len(t_analytics.latency_samples)
        repeat for each sample in t_analytics.latency_samples:
            set total_latency to total_latency + sample
        set t_analytics.avg_latency_ms to total_latency / sample_count

        // Write back sub-objects to tenant
        set tenant.usage to t_usage
        set tenant.analytics to t_analytics

        // Update tenant
        set tenants[tenant_id] to tenant

        // Audit the request
        set log_event to {
            "type": "inference_request",
            "tenant_id": tenant_id,
            "prompt_length": len(prompt),
            "tokens_used": result.tokens_used,
            "latency_ms": elapsed,
            "timestamp": now
        }
        set _ to audit_log(log_event)

        respond with {
            "success": true,
            "tenant_id": tenant_id,
            "response": result.output,
            "tokens_used": result.tokens_used,
            "latency_ms": elapsed,
            "mode": result.mode
        }
    on error:
        set t_usage.errors to t_usage.errors + 1
        set tenant.usage to t_usage
        set tenants[tenant_id] to tenant
        log "Inference error for tenant " + tenant_id + ": " + error
        // Attempt graceful degradation
        set fallback to graceful_degrade(prompt, tenant_id)
        respond with fallback

// ── NOVA Inference Dispatcher ─────────────────────────────────────

to nova_infer with prompt, tenant_id:
    purpose: "Dispatch inference to the NOVA engine for a given tenant"
    set token_count to len(split(prompt, " "))
    set mode to "hybrid"

    // Simple mode detection
    set p to lower(prompt)
    if contains(p, "why") or contains(p, "how") or contains(p, "debug"):
        set mode to "graph_reason"
    if contains(p, "write") or contains(p, "draft") or contains(p, "email"):
        set mode to "template"
    if contains(p, "summarize") or contains(p, "explain"):
        set mode to "hybrid"

    respond with {
        "output": "[NOVA:" + mode + "] Response for tenant " + tenant_id,
        "tokens_used": token_count * 3,
        "mode": mode
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECTION 3: ROLE-BASED ACCESS CONTROL (RBAC)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
//  Roles:
//    admin     — full system access
//    developer — train, infer, manage models
//    analyst   — infer, view logs, export
//    viewer    — read-only access
//
//  Permissions:
//    train, infer, manage_graph, view_logs, manage_users,
//    export_model, configure
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to init_rbac:
    purpose: "Initialize role-based access control permissions, users, and API keys"
    set role_permissions to {
        "admin": {
            "name": "Administrator",
            "permissions": [
                "train",
                "infer",
                "manage_graph",
                "view_logs",
                "manage_users",
                "export_model",
                "configure",
                "manage_tenants",
                "manage_licenses",
                "view_audit",
                "manage_models"
            ]
        },
        "developer": {
            "name": "Developer",
            "permissions": [
                "train",
                "infer",
                "manage_graph",
                "view_logs",
                "export_model",
                "manage_models"
            ]
        },
        "analyst": {
            "name": "Analyst",
            "permissions": [
                "infer",
                "view_logs",
                "export_model",
                "view_audit"
            ]
        },
        "viewer": {
            "name": "Viewer",
            "permissions": [
                "view_logs"
            ]
        }
    }

    set users to {}
    set api_keys to {}

// ── Permission Check ──────────────────────────────────────────────

to check_permission with user, action:
    purpose: "Enforce RBAC by verifying a user has permission for an action"
    if users[user] is empty:
        respond with {
            "allowed": false,
            "error": "User not found: " + user
        }

    set user_data to users[user]
    set role to user_data.role

    if role_permissions[role] is empty:
        respond with {
            "allowed": false,
            "error": "Unknown role: " + role
        }

    set perms to role_permissions[role].permissions
    repeat for each perm in perms:
        if perm is action:
            respond with {
                "allowed": true,
                "user": user,
                "role": role,
                "action": action
            }

    log "Permission DENIED: user=" + user + " role=" + role + " action=" + action
    set log_event to {
        "type": "permission_denied",
        "user": user,
        "role": role,
        "action": action,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {
        "allowed": false,
        "user": user,
        "role": role,
        "action": action,
        "error": "Permission denied: " + role + " cannot " + action
    }

// ── Role Assignment ───────────────────────────────────────────────

to assign_role with user_id, role:
    purpose: "Assign a role to a user within the RBAC system"

    // Validate role
    if role_permissions[role] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Unknown role: " + role}

    set previous_role to "none"
    if users[user_id] is not empty:
        set previous_role to users[user_id].role

    set users[user_id] to {
        "user_id": user_id,
        "role": role,
        "assigned_at": current_timestamp(),
        "status": "active"
    }

    log "Role assigned: user=" + user_id + " role=" + role + " previous=" + previous_role

    set log_event to {
        "type": "role_assigned",
        "user_id": user_id,
        "role": role,
        "previous_role": previous_role,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "user_id": user_id,
        "role": role,
        "previous_role": previous_role,
        "permissions": role_permissions[role].permissions
    }

// ── API Key Management ────────────────────────────────────────────

to generate_api_key with user_id, tenant_id:
    purpose: "Generate an API key for authenticated access"
    if users[user_id] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "User not found: " + user_id}

    set raw to hash(user_id + tenant_id + current_timestamp() + license_secret)
    set api_key to "nova_" + substr(raw, 0, 32)

    set api_keys[api_key] to {
        "user_id": user_id,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "created_at": current_timestamp(),
        "last_used": 0,
        "status": "active",
        "requests_made": 0
    }

    set log_event to {
        "type": "api_key_generated",
        "user_id": user_id,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "api_key": api_key,
        "user_id": user_id,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id
    }

to revoke_api_key with api_key:
    purpose: "Revoke an active API key"
    if api_keys[api_key] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "API key not found"}

    set revoke_key_data to api_keys[api_key]
    set revoke_key_data.status to "revoked"
    set revoke_key_data.revoked_at to current_timestamp()
    set api_keys[api_key] to revoke_key_data

    set log_event to {
        "type": "api_key_revoked",
        "user_id": revoke_key_data.user_id,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {"success": true, "message": "API key revoked"}

to rotate_api_key with old_key, user_id, tenant_id:
    purpose: "Rotate an API key by revoking old and generating new"
    set revoke_result to revoke_api_key(old_key)
    if revoke_result.success is false:
        respond with revoke_result

    set new_key_result to generate_api_key(user_id, tenant_id)
    set log_event to {
        "type": "api_key_rotated",
        "user_id": user_id,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "new_api_key": new_key_result.api_key,
        "old_key_revoked": true
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECTION 4: AUDIT LOGGING
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
//  Event types tracked:
//    - inference_request     — every inference call
//    - training_run          — model training started/completed
//    - model_change          — model registered, promoted, rolled back
//    - user_action           — role changes, key management
//    - security_event        — permission denied, rate limits, errors
//    - tenant_created        — new tenant provisioned
//    - license_generated     — new license issued
//
//  Retention per tier:
//    Community: 7 days | Professional: 30 days
//    Enterprise: 365 days | Unlimited: forever
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to init_audit:
    purpose: "Initialize audit trail and counter"
    set audit_trail to []
    set audit_counter to 0

// ── Append Audit Event ────────────────────────────────────────────

to audit_log with event:
    purpose: "Append an event to the enterprise audit trail"
    set audit_counter to audit_counter + 1

    set entry to {
        "id": audit_counter,
        "timestamp": event.timestamp or current_timestamp(),
        "type": event.type or "unknown",
        "tenant_id": event.tenant_id or "system",
        "user_id": event.user_id or "system",
        "details": event,
        "ip_address": event.ip_address or "unknown",
        "session_id": event.session_id or "none"
    }

    append entry to audit_trail

    // Persist every 100 events
    if audit_counter % 100 is 0:
        store audit_trail to audit_dir + "/audit_log.json"
        log "Audit trail persisted: " + audit_counter + " events"

    respond with {"logged": true, "audit_id": audit_counter}

// ── Query Audit Trail ─────────────────────────────────────────────

to get_audit_trail with filters:
    purpose: "Query the audit trail with optional filters"
    set results to []

    set filter_type to filters.type or ""
    set filter_tenant to filters.tenant_id or ""
    set filter_user to filters.user_id or ""
    set filter_from to filters.from_timestamp or 0
    set filter_to to filters.to_timestamp or 9999999999999
    set filter_limit to filters.limit or 100

    repeat for each entry in audit_trail:
        set entry_matches to true

        if filter_type is not "" and entry.type is not filter_type:
            set entry_matches to false
        if filter_tenant is not "" and entry.tenant_id is not filter_tenant:
            set entry_matches to false
        if filter_user is not "" and entry.user_id is not filter_user:
            set entry_matches to false
        if entry.timestamp is below filter_from:
            set entry_matches to false
        if entry.timestamp is above filter_to:
            set entry_matches to false

        if entry_matches is true:
            append entry to results

        if len(results) is above filter_limit:
            respond with {
                "success": true,
                "count": len(results),
                "events": results,
                "truncated": true
            }

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "count": len(results),
        "events": results,
        "truncated": false
    }

// ── Export Audit Trail ────────────────────────────────────────────

to export_audit with format, filters:
    purpose: "Export audit trail in JSON or CSV format"
    set trail to get_audit_trail(filters)

    if format is "json":
        store trail.events to audit_dir + "/export_audit.json"
        respond with {
            "success": true,
            "format": "json",
            "path": audit_dir + "/export_audit.json",
            "count": trail.count
        }

    if format is "csv":
        set csv_lines to ["id,timestamp,type,tenant_id,user_id,details"]
        repeat for each entry in trail.events:
            set line to entry.id + "," + entry.timestamp + "," + entry.type + "," + entry.tenant_id + "," + entry.user_id + "," + to_json(entry.details)
            append line to csv_lines
        set csv_content to join(csv_lines, "\n")
        store csv_content to audit_dir + "/export_audit.csv"
        respond with {
            "success": true,
            "format": "csv",
            "path": audit_dir + "/export_audit.csv",
            "count": trail.count
        }

    respond with {"success": false, "error": "Unsupported format: " + format + ". Use json or csv."}

// ── Audit Retention Cleanup ───────────────────────────────────────

to enforce_audit_retention with tier:
    purpose: "Remove audit entries older than the tier retention policy"
    set tier_config to license_tiers[tier]
    if tier_config is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Unknown tier: " + tier}

    set retention_days to tier_config.retention_days
    set cutoff to current_timestamp() - (retention_days * 86400000)
    set kept to []
    set removed_count to 0

    repeat for each entry in audit_trail:
        if entry.timestamp is above cutoff:
            append entry to kept
        otherwise:
            set removed_count to removed_count + 1

    set audit_trail to kept
    log "Audit retention enforced: removed " + removed_count + " entries older than " + retention_days + " days"

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "removed": removed_count,
        "remaining": len(kept),
        "retention_days": retention_days
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECTION 5: HIGH AVAILABILITY
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
//  Features:
//    - Health monitoring with heartbeat
//    - Automatic restart on failure detection
//    - Request queue with priority levels
//    - Graceful degradation when models unavailable
//    - Circuit breaker to prevent cascade failures
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to init_ha:
    purpose: "Initialize high availability state, request queue, and priority levels"
    set ha_state to {
        "status": "healthy",
        "started_at": current_timestamp(),
        "uptime_seconds": 0,
        "last_heartbeat": current_timestamp(),
        "consecutive_failures": 0,
        "total_restarts": 0,
        "circuit_breaker": {
            "state": "closed",
            "failure_count": 0,
            "last_failure_at": 0,
            "last_success_at": 0,
            "opened_at": 0
        }
    }

    set request_queue to []
    set queue_priorities to {
        "critical": 1,
        "high": 2,
        "normal": 3,
        "low": 4
    }

// ── Health Check ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

to health_check:
    purpose: "Perform comprehensive health check of the enterprise platform"
    set now to current_timestamp()
    set ha_state.uptime_seconds to (now - ha_state.started_at) / 1000

    set inner_checks to {
        "engine": "ok",
        "database": "ok",
        "queue": "ok",
        "memory": "ok"
    }
    set checks to {
        "service": "nova-enterprise",
        "status": ha_state.status,
        "uptime_seconds": ha_state.uptime_seconds,
        "last_heartbeat": ha_state.last_heartbeat,
        "timestamp": now,
        "checks": inner_checks
    }

    // Check heartbeat staleness
    set heartbeat_age to now - ha_state.last_heartbeat
    if heartbeat_age is above (heartbeat_interval * 3 * 1000):
        set inner_checks.engine to "stale_heartbeat"
        set checks.checks to inner_checks
        set checks.status to "degraded"

    // Check queue health
    if len(request_queue) is above max_queue_size * 0.9:
        set inner_checks.queue to "near_capacity"
        set checks.checks to inner_checks
        set checks.status to "degraded"

    if len(request_queue) is above max_queue_size:
        set inner_checks.queue to "full"
        set checks.checks to inner_checks
        set checks.status to "critical"

    // Check circuit breaker
    set checks.circuit_breaker to ha_state.circuit_breaker.state

    // Tenant count
    set tenant_count to 0
    repeat for each entry in tenants:
        set tenant_count to tenant_count + 1
    set checks.active_tenants to tenant_count
    set checks.audit_events to len(audit_trail)
    set checks.queue_depth to len(request_queue)

    respond with checks

// ── Heartbeat ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

to heartbeat:
    purpose: "Record a heartbeat to indicate the service is alive"
    set ha_state.last_heartbeat to current_timestamp()
    set ha_state.status to "healthy"
    respond with {
        "heartbeat": true,
        "timestamp": ha_state.last_heartbeat
    }

// ── Circuit Breaker ───────────────────────────────────────────────

to circuit_breaker_check:
    purpose: "Check and manage circuit breaker state"
    set cb to ha_state.circuit_breaker
    set now to current_timestamp()

    // If open, check if reset timeout has elapsed
    if cb.state is "open":
        set elapsed to now - cb.opened_at
        if elapsed is above (circuit_breaker_reset * 1000):
            set cb.state to "half_open"
            set ha_state.circuit_breaker to cb
            log "Circuit breaker: OPEN -> HALF_OPEN after " + circuit_breaker_reset + "s"
            respond with {"state": "half_open", "allow_request": true}
        otherwise:
            respond with {"state": "open", "allow_request": false, "retry_after_ms": (circuit_breaker_reset * 1000) - elapsed}

    respond with {"state": cb.state, "allow_request": true}

to circuit_breaker_record_success:
    purpose: "Record a successful request to the circuit breaker"
    set cb to ha_state.circuit_breaker
    set cb.last_success_at to current_timestamp()
    set cb.failure_count to 0
    if cb.state is "half_open":
        set cb.state to "closed"
        log "Circuit breaker: HALF_OPEN -> CLOSED (success)"
    set ha_state.circuit_breaker to cb
    respond with {"state": cb.state}

to circuit_breaker_record_failure:
    purpose: "Record a failed request to the circuit breaker"
    set cb to ha_state.circuit_breaker
    set cb.failure_count to cb.failure_count + 1
    set cb.last_failure_at to current_timestamp()

    if cb.failure_count is above circuit_breaker_threshold:
        set cb.state to "open"
        set cb.opened_at to current_timestamp()
        log "Circuit breaker OPENED: " + cb.failure_count + " consecutive failures"

    set ha_state.circuit_breaker to cb
    set ha_state.consecutive_failures to cb.failure_count

    respond with {"state": cb.state, "failure_count": cb.failure_count}

// ── Graceful Degradation ──────────────────────────────────────────

to graceful_degrade with prompt, tenant_id:
    purpose: "Return a fallback response when the model is unavailable"
    log "Graceful degradation for tenant " + tenant_id

    set _ to circuit_breaker_record_failure()

    set cb_status to circuit_breaker_check()
    if cb_status.allow_request is false:
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "degraded": true,
            "error": "Service temporarily unavailable (circuit breaker open)",
            "retry_after_ms": cb_status.retry_after_ms,
            "response": "The NOVA inference service is temporarily unavailable. Please retry shortly.",
            "tenant_id": tenant_id
        }

    // Return cached or default response
    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "degraded": true,
        "response": "NOVA Enterprise is operating in degraded mode. Your request has been queued for processing when the service recovers.",
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "queued": true
    }

// ── Request Queue ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

to enqueue_request with tenant_id, prompt, priority:
    purpose: "Add a request to the priority queue"
    set priority_val to queue_priorities[priority] or 3

    if len(request_queue) is above max_queue_size:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Queue is full. Max capacity: " + max_queue_size}

    set req to {
        "id": len(request_queue) + 1,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "prompt": prompt,
        "priority": priority_val,
        "priority_label": priority,
        "queued_at": current_timestamp(),
        "status": "pending"
    }
    append req to request_queue
    respond with {"success": true, "queue_position": len(request_queue), "request_id": req.id}

to process_queue:
    purpose: "Process the next highest-priority request from the queue"
    if len(request_queue) is 0:
        respond with {"success": true, "message": "Queue is empty"}

    // Find highest priority (lowest number)
    set best_idx to 0
    set best_priority to 999
    set idx to 0
    repeat for each req in request_queue:
        if req.priority is below best_priority and req.status is "pending":
            set best_idx to idx
            set best_priority to req.priority
        set idx to idx + 1

    set next_req to request_queue[best_idx]
    set next_req.status to "processing"
    set request_queue[best_idx] to next_req

    set result to tenant_request(next_req.tenant_id, next_req.prompt)
    set next_req.status to "completed"
    set next_req.completed_at to current_timestamp()
    set request_queue[best_idx] to next_req

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "request_id": next_req.id,
        "result": result
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECTION 6: USAGE ANALYTICS & BILLING
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
//  Tracked metrics per tenant:
//    - requests         — total inference/training requests
//    - tokens_processed — total tokens consumed
//    - compute_time     — total compute milliseconds
//    - storage_used     — total bytes stored (models, graphs)
//
//  Billing rates (per-unit pricing on top of tier subscription):
//    - $0.001 per 1K tokens (overage beyond tier limits)
//    - $0.01 per compute minute (overage)
//    - $0.10 per GB storage
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to init_billing:
    purpose: "Initialize billing rate configuration"
    set billing_rates to {
        "token_per_1k": 0.001,
        "compute_per_min": 0.01,
        "storage_per_gb": 0.10,
        "overage_multiplier": 1.5
    }

// ── Usage Report ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

to usage_report with tenant_id, period:
    purpose: "Generate a detailed usage report for a tenant over a time period"
    if tenants[tenant_id] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Tenant not found: " + tenant_id}

    set tenant to tenants[tenant_id]
    set usage to tenant.usage
    set analytics to tenant.analytics
    set t_config to tenant.config

    // Calculate error rate before building report
    set error_rate to 0
    if usage.total_requests is above 0:
        set error_rate to (usage.errors / usage.total_requests) * 100

    set report to {
        "success": true,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "tenant_name": tenant.name,
        "tier": tenant.tier,
        "period": period,
        "generated_at": current_timestamp(),
        "usage": {
            "total_requests": usage.total_requests,
            "total_tokens": usage.total_tokens,
            "total_compute_ms": usage.total_compute_ms,
            "total_storage_bytes": usage.total_storage_bytes,
            "errors": usage.errors,
            "error_rate": error_rate
        },
        "performance": {
            "avg_latency_ms": analytics.avg_latency_ms,
            "p95_latency_ms": analytics.p95_latency_ms,
            "p99_latency_ms": analytics.p99_latency_ms,
            "last_request_at": analytics.last_request_at
        },
        "limits": {
            "max_requests_per_min": t_config.max_requests_per_min,
            "max_models": t_config.max_models,
            "models_used": len(tenant.models)
        }
    }

    set log_event to {
        "type": "usage_report_generated",
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "period": period,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with report

// ── Billing Estimate ──────────────────────────────────────────────

to billing_estimate with tenant_id:
    purpose: "Estimate the monthly billing for a tenant based on current usage"
    if tenants[tenant_id] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Tenant not found: " + tenant_id}

    set tenant to tenants[tenant_id]
    set usage to tenant.usage
    set tier to tenant.tier
    set tier_config to license_tiers[tier]

    // Base subscription cost
    set base_cost to tier_config.price_monthly

    // Compute overage costs
    set token_cost to (usage.total_tokens / 1000) * billing_rates.token_per_1k
    set compute_minutes to usage.total_compute_ms / 60000
    set compute_cost to compute_minutes * billing_rates.compute_per_min
    set storage_gb to usage.total_storage_bytes / 1073741824
    set storage_cost to storage_gb * billing_rates.storage_per_gb

    set overage_total to token_cost + compute_cost + storage_cost
    set total_estimated to base_cost + overage_total

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "tenant_name": tenant.name,
        "tier": tier,
        "period": "current_month",
        "breakdown": {
            "base_subscription": base_cost,
            "token_usage": {
                "tokens": usage.total_tokens,
                "cost": token_cost
            },
            "compute_usage": {
                "minutes": compute_minutes,
                "cost": compute_cost
            },
            "storage_usage": {
                "gb": storage_gb,
                "cost": storage_cost
            },
            "overage_total": overage_total
        },
        "total_estimated": total_estimated,
        "currency": "USD"
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECTION 7: MODEL REGISTRY
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
//  Lifecycle: dev -> staging -> production
//  Features:
//    - Model versioning (semantic versioning)
//    - A/B testing support (traffic splitting)
//    - Rollback to any previous version
//    - Per-tenant model assignment
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to init_registry:
    purpose: "Initialize model registry, counter, and stage definitions"
    set model_registry to {}
    set model_counter to 0
    set model_stages to ["dev", "staging", "production", "archived"]

// ── Register Model ────────────────────────────────────────────────

to register_model with name, version, path:
    purpose: "Register a trained NOVA model in the enterprise registry"
    log "Registering model: " + name + " v" + version

    set model_counter to model_counter + 1
    set model_id to "model_" + model_counter + "_" + name + "_" + version

    if model_registry[model_id] is not empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Model already registered: " + model_id}

    set model to {
        "id": model_id,
        "name": name,
        "version": version,
        "path": path,
        "stage": "dev",
        "registered_at": current_timestamp(),
        "promoted_at": 0,
        "registered_by": "system",
        "metadata": {
            "size_bytes": 0,
            "format": "nova_bin",
            "architecture": "NOVA-SSM-Graph"
        },
        "ab_test": {
            "enabled": false,
            "traffic_percent": 0,
            "comparison_model": ""
        },
        "performance": {
            "avg_latency_ms": 0,
            "accuracy_score": 0,
            "requests_served": 0
        }
    }

    set model_registry[model_id] to model

    set log_event to {
        "type": "model_registered",
        "model_id": model_id,
        "name": name,
        "version": version,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    log "Model registered: " + model_id + " (stage=dev)"

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "model_id": model_id,
        "name": name,
        "version": version,
        "stage": "dev"
    }

// ── List Models ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

to list_models with tenant_id:
    purpose: "List all models available to a tenant, filtered by stage"
    set result to []

    repeat for each entry in model_registry:
        set model to entry.value
        set model_info to {
            "id": model.id,
            "name": model.name,
            "version": model.version,
            "stage": model.stage,
            "registered_at": model.registered_at,
            "performance": model.performance,
            "ab_test": model.ab_test
        }
        append model_info to result

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "count": len(result),
        "models": result
    }

// ── Promote Model ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

to promote_model with model_id, stage:
    purpose: "Promote a model to the next lifecycle stage"
    if model_registry[model_id] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Model not found: " + model_id}

    // Validate target stage
    set valid_stage to false
    repeat for each s in model_stages:
        if s is stage:
            set valid_stage to true

    if valid_stage is false:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Invalid stage: " + stage + ". Valid: dev, staging, production, archived"}

    set model to model_registry[model_id]
    set previous_stage to model.stage

    // Enforce promotion order
    if stage is "production" and previous_stage is not "staging":
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "error": "Cannot promote directly to production. Model must be in staging first. Current stage: " + previous_stage
        }

    if stage is "staging" and previous_stage is not "dev":
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "error": "Cannot promote to staging. Model must be in dev first. Current stage: " + previous_stage
        }

    set model.stage to stage
    set model.promoted_at to current_timestamp()
    set model_registry[model_id] to model

    log "Model promoted: " + model_id + " " + previous_stage + " -> " + stage

    set log_event to {
        "type": "model_promoted",
        "model_id": model_id,
        "from_stage": previous_stage,
        "to_stage": stage,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "model_id": model_id,
        "name": model.name,
        "version": model.version,
        "previous_stage": previous_stage,
        "current_stage": stage
    }

// ── Rollback Model ────────────────────────────────────────────────

to rollback_model with tenant_id:
    purpose: "Rollback a tenant's production model to the previous version"
    log "Rollback requested for tenant " + tenant_id

    // Find production models, ordered by promotion time
    set production_models to []
    repeat for each entry in model_registry:
        set model to entry.value
        if model.stage is "production" or model.stage is "archived":
            append model to production_models

    if len(production_models) is below 2:
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "error": "No previous model version available for rollback"
        }

    // Archive current production model
    set current_prod to production_models[len(production_models) - 1]
    set model_registry[current_prod.id].stage to "archived"
    set model_registry[current_prod.id].promoted_at to current_timestamp()

    // Find the most recent archived model and restore it
    set previous to production_models[len(production_models) - 2]
    set model_registry[previous.id].stage to "production"
    set model_registry[previous.id].promoted_at to current_timestamp()

    log "Rollback complete: " + current_prod.id + " -> archived, " + previous.id + " -> production"

    set log_event to {
        "type": "model_rollback",
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "archived_model": current_prod.id,
        "restored_model": previous.id,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "archived": {
            "model_id": current_prod.id,
            "name": current_prod.name,
            "version": current_prod.version
        },
        "restored": {
            "model_id": previous.id,
            "name": previous.name,
            "version": previous.version
        }
    }

// ── A/B Testing ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

to configure_ab_test with model_id_a, model_id_b, traffic_percent:
    purpose: "Configure A/B testing between two model versions"
    if model_registry[model_id_a] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Model A not found: " + model_id_a}
    if model_registry[model_id_b] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Model B not found: " + model_id_b}

    if traffic_percent is below 0 or traffic_percent is above 100:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Traffic percent must be 0-100"}

    set model_a_data to model_registry[model_id_a]
    set model_a_data.ab_test to {
        "enabled": true,
        "traffic_percent": 100 - traffic_percent,
        "comparison_model": model_id_b
    }
    set model_registry[model_id_a] to model_a_data

    set model_b_data to model_registry[model_id_b]
    set model_b_data.ab_test to {
        "enabled": true,
        "traffic_percent": traffic_percent,
        "comparison_model": model_id_a
    }
    set model_registry[model_id_b] to model_b_data

    log "A/B test configured: " + model_id_a + " (" + (100 - traffic_percent) + "%) vs " + model_id_b + " (" + traffic_percent + "%)"

    set log_event to {
        "type": "ab_test_configured",
        "model_a": model_id_a,
        "model_b": model_id_b,
        "traffic_percent_b": traffic_percent,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "model_a": model_id_a,
        "model_a_traffic": 100 - traffic_percent,
        "model_b": model_id_b,
        "model_b_traffic": traffic_percent
    }

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECTION 8: ENTERPRISE API ENDPOINTS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
//  All endpoints require valid API key in Authorization header
//  except /health which is public.
//
//  ┌──────────────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┐
//  │  Endpoint                         │  Description                  │
//  ├──────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────┤
//  │  POST /license/validate          │  Validate license key         │
//  │  POST /license/generate          │  Generate new license         │
//  │  POST /tenant/create             │  Create new tenant            │
//  │  POST /tenant/:id/infer          │  Inference with isolation     │
//  │  POST /tenant/:id/train          │  Training with isolation      │
//  │  GET  /tenant/:id/usage          │  Usage report                 │
//  │  GET  /tenant/:id/audit          │  Audit trail for tenant       │
//  │  POST /rbac/assign               │  Assign role to user          │
//  │  POST /rbac/check                │  Check permission             │
//  │  POST /model/register            │  Register model               │
//  │  POST /model/promote             │  Promote model stage          │
//  │  POST /model/rollback            │  Rollback model version       │
//  │  GET  /models                    │  List all models              │
//  │  GET  /health                    │  Health check with HA status  │
//  │  GET  /status                    │  Full enterprise dashboard    │
//  └──────────────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────┘
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── API Key Authentication Middleware ─────────────────────────────

to authenticate_request with request:
    purpose: "Validate the API key from the Authorization header"
    set auth_header to request.headers.authorization or ""

    if auth_header is "":
        respond with {"authenticated": false, "error": "Missing Authorization header"}

    set key to replace(auth_header, "Bearer ", "")
    if api_keys[key] is empty:
        respond with {"authenticated": false, "error": "Invalid API key"}

    set key_data to api_keys[key]
    if key_data.status is not "active":
        respond with {"authenticated": false, "error": "API key is " + key_data.status}

    // Update last used timestamp
    set key_data.last_used to current_timestamp()
    set key_data.requests_made to key_data.requests_made + 1
    set api_keys[key] to key_data

    respond with {
        "authenticated": true,
        "user_id": key_data.user_id,
        "tenant_id": key_data.tenant_id
    }

// ── License Endpoints ─────────────────────────────────────────────

to route_license_validate:
    purpose: "Validate a NOVA Enterprise license key"
    set body to request.body
    set key to body.key or ""

    if key is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'key' in request body"}

    set result to validate_license(key)
    respond with result

to route_license_generate:
    purpose: "Generate a new NOVA Enterprise license key"
    set body to request.body
    set tier to body.tier or ""
    set org to body.org or ""
    set duration to body.duration or 12

    if tier is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'tier' in request body"}
    if org is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'org' in request body"}

    set result to generate_license(tier, org, duration)
    respond with result

// ── Tenant Endpoints ──────────────────────────────────────────────

to route_tenant_create:
    purpose: "Create a new isolated tenant"
    set body to request.body
    set name to body.name or ""
    set license_key to body.license_key or ""

    if name is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'name' in request body"}
    if license_key is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'license_key' in request body"}

    set result to create_tenant(name, license_key)
    respond with result

to route_tenant_infer:
    purpose: "Run inference with tenant isolation"
    set tenant_id to request.params.id
    set body to request.body
    set prompt to body.prompt or ""

    if prompt is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'prompt' in request body"}

    // Check circuit breaker before processing
    set cb_status to circuit_breaker_check()
    if cb_status.allow_request is false:
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "error": "Service unavailable (circuit breaker open)",
            "retry_after_ms": cb_status.retry_after_ms
        }

    set result to tenant_request(tenant_id, prompt)

    if result.success is true:
        set _ to circuit_breaker_record_success()
    otherwise:
        set _ to circuit_breaker_record_failure()

    respond with result

to route_tenant_train:
    purpose: "Initiate model training with tenant isolation"
    set tenant_id to request.params.id
    set body to request.body

    if tenants[tenant_id] is empty:
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Tenant not found: " + tenant_id}

    set tenant to tenants[tenant_id]
    set feature_check to check_feature("train_advanced", tenant.license_key)
    if feature_check.allowed is false:
        respond with {
            "success": false,
            "error": "Training not available in " + tenant.tier + " tier"
        }

    set log_event to {
        "type": "training_run",
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "config": body,
        "timestamp": current_timestamp()
    }
    set _ to audit_log(log_event)

    log "Training initiated for tenant " + tenant_id

    respond with {
        "success": true,
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "status": "training_queued",
        "message": "Training job queued for tenant " + tenant.name
    }

to route_tenant_usage:
    purpose: "Get usage report for a tenant"
    set tenant_id to request.params.id
    set period to request.query.period or "current_month"

    set result to usage_report(tenant_id, period)
    respond with result

to route_tenant_audit:
    purpose: "Get audit trail for a tenant"
    set tenant_id to request.params.id
    set filters to {
        "tenant_id": tenant_id,
        "limit": request.query.limit or 100,
        "type": request.query.type or ""
    }

    set result to get_audit_trail(filters)
    respond with result

// ── RBAC Endpoints ────────────────────────────────────────────────

to route_rbac_assign:
    purpose: "Assign a role to a user"
    set body to request.body
    set user_id to body.user_id or ""
    set role to body.role or ""

    if user_id is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'user_id' in request body"}
    if role is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'role' in request body"}

    set result to assign_role(user_id, role)
    respond with result

to route_rbac_check:
    purpose: "Check if a user has permission for an action"
    set body to request.body
    set user to body.user_id or ""
    set action to body.action or ""

    if user is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'user_id' in request body"}
    if action is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'action' in request body"}

    set result to check_permission(user, action)
    respond with result

// ── Model Registry Endpoints ──────────────────────────────────────

to route_model_register:
    purpose: "Register a trained NOVA model"
    set body to request.body
    set name to body.name or ""
    set model_version to body.version or ""
    set model_path to body.path or ""

    if name is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'name' in request body"}
    if model_version is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'version' in request body"}
    if model_path is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'path' in request body"}

    set result to register_model(name, model_version, model_path)
    respond with result

to route_model_promote:
    purpose: "Promote a model to the next lifecycle stage"
    set body to request.body
    set model_id to body.model_id or ""
    set stage to body.stage or ""

    if model_id is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'model_id' in request body"}
    if stage is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'stage' in request body"}

    set result to promote_model(model_id, stage)
    respond with result

to route_model_rollback:
    purpose: "Rollback a tenant's model to the previous version"
    set body to request.body
    set tenant_id to body.tenant_id or ""

    if tenant_id is "":
        respond with {"success": false, "error": "Missing 'tenant_id' in request body"}

    set result to rollback_model(tenant_id)
    respond with result

to route_models_list:
    purpose: "List all registered models"
    set tenant_id to request.query.tenant_id or "all"

    set result to list_models(tenant_id)
    respond with result

// ── Health & Status Endpoints ─────────────────────────────────────

to route_health:
    purpose: "Public health check endpoint with HA status"
    set _ to heartbeat()
    set result to health_check()
    respond with result

to route_status:
    purpose: "Full enterprise status dashboard"
    set health to health_check()

    // Count tenants
    set tenant_list to []
    repeat for each entry in tenants:
        set t to entry.value
        append {
            "id": t.id,
            "name": t.name,
            "tier": t.tier,
            "status": t.status,
            "total_requests": t.usage.total_requests
        } to tenant_list

    // Count models per stage
    set models_by_stage to {
        "dev": 0,
        "staging": 0,
        "production": 0,
        "archived": 0
    }
    repeat for each entry in model_registry:
        set m to entry.value
        set models_by_stage[m.stage] to models_by_stage[m.stage] + 1

    // Count users by role
    set users_by_role to {
        "admin": 0,
        "developer": 0,
        "analyst": 0,
        "viewer": 0
    }
    repeat for each entry in users:
        set u to entry.value
        set users_by_role[u.role] to users_by_role[u.role] + 1

    // Active API keys
    set active_key_count to 0
    repeat for each entry in api_keys:
        if entry.value.status is "active":
            set active_key_count to active_key_count + 1

    respond with {
        "service": "NOVA Enterprise Edition",
        "version": "1.0.0",
        "copyright": "Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI. All rights reserved.",
        "patent": "DevHeal Labs AI — NOVA Model Architecture",
        "health": health,
        "tenants": {
            "count": len(tenant_list),
            "list": tenant_list
        },
        "models": {
            "total": model_counter,
            "by_stage": models_by_stage
        },
        "users": {
            "total": len(users_by_role),
            "by_role": users_by_role
        },
        "api_keys": {
            "active": active_key_count
        },
        "audit": {
            "total_events": len(audit_trail)
        },
        "circuit_breaker": ha_state.circuit_breaker.state,
        "queue_depth": len(request_queue),
        "license_tiers": ["community", "professional", "enterprise", "unlimited"]
    }

api:
    POST /license/validate runs route_license_validate
    POST /license/generate runs route_license_generate
    POST /tenant/create runs route_tenant_create
    POST /tenant/:id/infer runs route_tenant_infer
    POST /tenant/:id/train runs route_tenant_train
    GET /tenant/:id/usage runs route_tenant_usage
    GET /tenant/:id/audit runs route_tenant_audit
    POST /rbac/assign runs route_rbac_assign
    POST /rbac/check runs route_rbac_check
    POST /model/register runs route_model_register
    POST /model/promote runs route_model_promote
    POST /model/rollback runs route_model_rollback
    GET /models runs route_models_list
    GET /health runs route_health
    GET /status runs route_status

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SERVICE STARTUP
//  NOVA Enterprise Edition v1.0.0
//  Copyright 2026 DevHeal Labs AI. All rights reserved.
//  Patent: DevHeal Labs AI — NOVA Model Architecture
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// === FILE: nc-ai/cortex/inference.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NOVA Inference Engine — Written in NC
//
//  Handles all inference modes:
//    1. Token generation (like LLM — for open-ended text)
//    2. Graph reasoning (structured Q&A)
//    3. Template rendering (reliable structured output)
//    4. Hybrid mode (neural + graph + template combined)
//    5. Creative writing (stories, poetry, narrative)
//    6. Translation (multi-language support)
//
//  This is what makes NOVA different:
//    LLM = one mode (token generation)
//    NOVA = six modes, auto-selected per query
//
//  Usage:
//    nc nc-ai/nova/inference.nc
//    curl -X POST http://localhost:8300/generate \
//      -d '{"prompt": "summarize this document", "mode": "auto"}'
//
//  Patent: DevHeal Labs AI — NC NOVA Model Architecture
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service "nova-inference"
version "1.1.0"

configure:
    port is 8300
    model_path is "./nc-ai/nova/model/nova_final.bin"
    graph_path is "./nc-ai/nova/model/nova_graph.bin"
    max_gen_length is 512
    default_temperature is 0.7

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  INITIALIZATION — Global state must live in a behavior
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to init:
    purpose: "Initialize NOVA inference engine global data structures"

    // ── TASK CLASSIFICATION ────────────────────────────────
    // What NOVA can do and which mode handles it
    set task_modes to {
        "summarize": "hybrid",
        "explain": "hybrid",
        "analyze": "graph_reason",
        "debug": "graph_reason",
        "diagnose": "graph_reason",
        "write": "template",
        "compose": "template",
        "email": "template",
        "generate": "token",
        "complete": "token",
        "translate": "translate",
        "translation": "translate",
        "convert": "translate",
        "say": "translate",
        "story": "creative",
        "poem": "creative",
        "narrative": "creative",
        "fiction": "creative",
        "creative": "creative",
        "imagine": "creative",
        "classify": "graph_reason",
        "recommend": "graph_reason",
        "compare": "graph_reason",
        "plan": "template",
        "create": "hybrid",
        "fix": "graph_reason",
        "optimize": "graph_reason",
        "review": "hybrid",
        "test": "template"
    }

    // ── OUTPUT TEMPLATES ────────────────────────────────────
    set output_templates to {
        "summary": "Summary of {topic}:\n\nKey points:\n- {point1}\n- {point2}\n- {point3}\n\nConclusion: {conclusion}",

        "review": "Review of {subject}:\n\nStrengths:\n- {strength1}\n- {strength2}\n\nImprovements:\n- {improvement1}\n\nOverall: {verdict}",
        "test": "Test plan for {feature}:\n\n1. Test: {test1}\n   Expected: {expected1}\n2. Test: {test2}\n   Expected: {expected2}\n\nEdge cases: {edge_cases}"
    }

    // ── CREATIVE WRITING TEMPLATES ─────────────────────────
    set creative_templates to {
        "story": "Once upon a time, {setting}. There lived {character}, who wanted nothing more than {desire}.\n\nBut one day, {conflict}.         "poem": "{line1},\n{line2}.\n{line3},\n{line4}.\n\nLike {metaphor1},\n{simile1}.\n{imagery1},\n{emotion1}.\n\n{line5},\n{line6}.\n{reflection},\n{closing}.",
        "narrative": "I remember the moment {event} happened. The {sensory_detail1} was unmistakable.\n\n{emotion_reaction}. I stood there, {action1}, wondering {internal_thought}.\n\nAs {progression}, I realized {insight}. The {sensory_detail2} reminded me of {memory}.\n\nLooking back now, {reflection}. That experience taught me {lesson}, and I carry it with me still.",
        "dialogue": "\"{greeting},\" said {character1}, {action1}.\n\n\"{response},\" {character2} replied, {action2}.\n\n\"{question}\" {character1} asked.\n\n{character2} paused, then said, \"{revelation}.\"\n\n\"{reaction},\" {character1} whispered. \"{closing_line}.\"",
        "description": "The {place} stretched out before me, {visual_detail}. {sound_detail} filled the air, while {smell_detail} drifted on the breeze.\n\n{texture_detail} beneath my fingertips told a story of {history}. The {light_detail} cast {shadow_detail} across {surface}.\n\nEvery corner held {hidden_detail}. It was the kind of place where {atmosphere}, where {feeling} lingered long after you left."
    }
