            set start to len(generated) - model_config.max_seq_len
            set generated to slice(generated, start, len(generated))

        // Forward pass
        set logits to forward(generated)

        // Get last token's logits
        set last_row_idx to len(logits) - 1
        set last_logits to get(logits, last_row_idx)

        // Apply temperature
        if temperature is above 0:
            set scaled to []
            repeat for each logit in last_logits:
                append logit / temperature to scaled
            set last_logits to scaled

        // Softmax to get probabilities
        set probs to tensor_softmax([last_logits])
        set probs to get(probs, 0)

        // Greedy sampling (argmax)
        set next_token to 0
        set best_prob to 0
        set i to 0
        repeat for each p in probs:
            if p is above best_prob:
                set best_prob to p
                set next_token to i
            set i to i + 1

        append next_token to generated

        // Stop on EOS token (id=2)
        if next_token is equal 2:
            set step to max_new_tokens

        set step to step + 1

    respond with generated

// ── Save / Load Model ────────────────────────────────────────

to save_model with path:
    purpose: "Save model weights to disk"
    log "Saving model to " + path + "..."
    tensor_save(token_embedding, path + "/token_emb.nct")
    tensor_save(pos_embedding, path + "/pos_emb.nct")
    tensor_save(lm_head, path + "/lm_head.nct")
    tensor_save(final_norm_gamma, path + "/final_norm_g.nct")
    tensor_save(final_norm_beta, path + "/final_norm_b.nct")

    set layer_idx to 0
    repeat while layer_idx is below model_config.num_layers:
        set layer to get(layers, layer_idx)
        set prefix to path + "/layer_" + string(layer_idx)
        tensor_save(layer.attn_q_weight, prefix + "_attn_q_w.nct")
        tensor_save(layer.attn_k_weight, prefix + "_attn_k_w.nct")
        tensor_save(layer.attn_v_weight, prefix + "_attn_v_w.nct")
        tensor_save(layer.attn_o_weight, prefix + "_attn_o_w.nct")
        tensor_save(layer.ff_up_weight, prefix + "_ff_up_w.nct")
        tensor_save(layer.ff_down_weight, prefix + "_ff_down_w.nct")
        set layer_idx to layer_idx + 1

    store model_config into path + "/config.json"
    log "Model saved to " + path
    respond with true

to load_model with path:
    purpose: "Load model weights from disk"
    log "Loading model from " + path + "..."

    gather config from path + "/config.json"
    if config is equal nil:
        log "No model found at " + path
        respond with false

    init_model(config)

    set token_embedding to tensor_load(path + "/token_emb.nct")
    set pos_embedding to tensor_load(path + "/pos_emb.nct")
    set lm_head to tensor_load(path + "/lm_head.nct")
    set final_norm_gamma to tensor_load(path + "/final_norm_g.nct")
    set final_norm_beta to tensor_load(path + "/final_norm_b.nct")

    set layer_idx to 0
    repeat while layer_idx is below config.num_layers:
        set prefix to path + "/layer_" + string(layer_idx)
        set layer to get(layers, layer_idx)
        set layer.attn_q_weight to tensor_load(prefix + "_attn_q_w.nct")
        set layer.attn_k_weight to tensor_load(prefix + "_attn_k_w.nct")
        set layer.attn_v_weight to tensor_load(prefix + "_attn_v_w.nct")
        set layer.attn_o_weight to tensor_load(prefix + "_attn_o_w.nct")
        set layer.ff_up_weight to tensor_load(prefix + "_ff_up_w.nct")
        set layer.ff_down_weight to tensor_load(prefix + "_ff_down_w.nct")
        set layer_idx to layer_idx + 1

    log "Model loaded from " + path
    respond with true

// ── Model Info ───────────────────────────────────────────────

to info:
    purpose: "Return model information"
    respond with {
        "name": "NC Transformer",
        "version": "2.0.0",
        "written_in": "NC Language (100%)",
        "engine": "NC tensor ops (C runtime)",
        "architecture": "decoder-only transformer (autoregressive)"
    }

api:
    POST /init       runs init_model
    POST /forward    runs forward
    POST /generate   runs generate
    POST /save       runs save_model
    POST /load       runs load_model
    GET  /info       runs info

// === FILE: nc-ai/nc/server.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NC AI Server — The Complete NC AI System
//
//  Written 100% in NC Language. The C engine provides only:
//    - VM (bytecode execution)
//    - Compiler (parse → bytecodes)
//    - Tensor math (matmul, gelu, softmax — via tensor_* functions)
//
//  Everything else — model, tokenizer, training, code gen — is NC.
//
//  Start: nc nc-ai/nc/server.nc
//  Port:  8090
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service "nc-ai"
version "2.0.0"

configure:
    port is 8090
    ai_model is "default"

// ── Intent Detection ────────────────────────────────────────

to detect_intent with prompt:
    purpose: "Classify the user request"
    set p to lower(prompt)
    set intent to "service"
    set features to []
    set name to "my-service"

    // Check intents from most specific to least specific
    if contains(p, "chat") or contains(p, "conversation") or contains(p, "chatbot"):
        set intent to "chatbot"
    if contains(p, "crud") or contains(p, "database"):
        set intent to "crud"
    if contains(p, "classify") or contains(p, "categorize"):
        set intent to "classifier"
    if contains(p, "summarize") or contains(p, "summary"):
        set intent to "summarizer"
    if contains(p, "pipeline") or contains(p, "etl"):
        set intent to "pipeline"
    if contains(p, "webhook") or contains(p, "hook"):
        set intent to "webhook"
    if contains(p, "dashboard") or contains(p, "frontend"):
        set intent to "ncui"
    if contains(p, "stock") or contains(p, "trading") or contains(p, "finance"):
        set intent to "finance"
    if contains(p, "monitor") or contains(p, "observability"):
        set intent to "monitoring"
    if contains(p, "auth") or contains(p, "jwt"):
        append "auth" to features
    if contains(p, "ai") or contains(p, "llm") or contains(p, "intelligent"):
        append "ai" to features
    if contains(p, "rate limit"):
        append "rate_limit" to features

    // Extract name from prompt
    set words to split(p, " ")
    repeat for each word in words:
        if len(word) is above 3:
            if word is not equal "create" and word is not equal "build" and word is not equal "make":
                if word is not equal "service" and word is not equal "with" and word is not equal "that":
                    if word is not equal "using" and word is not equal "from" and word is not equal "into":
                        set name to word

    respond with {"intent": intent, "features": features, "name": name}

// ── Template Engine ─────────────────────────────────────────

to generate_from_template with intent, name, features:
    purpose: "Generate NC code from templates"
    set has_ai to false
    repeat for each f in features:
        if f is equal "ai":
            set has_ai to true

    set q to chr(34)
    set nl to chr(10)
    set t to "    "
    set code to "service " + q + name + q + nl + "version " + q + "1.0.0" + q + nl

    if has_ai:
        set code to code + nl + "configure:" + nl + t + "ai_model is " + q + "default" + q + nl

    if intent is equal "crud":
        set code to code + nl + "to create with data:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "store data into " + q + name + q + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "created" + q + ": true, " + q + "data" + q + ": data}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to list_all:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "gather items from " + q + name + q + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with items" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to get_one with id:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "gather item from " + q + name + q + " where id" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with item" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to update with id, data:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "store data into " + q + name + q + " where id" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "updated" + q + ": true}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to delete_one with id:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "remove from " + q + name + q + " where id" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "deleted" + q + ": true}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to health:" + nl + t + "respond with {" + q + "status" + q + ": " + q + "ok" + q + "}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "POST   /" + name + "      runs create" + nl
        set code to code + t + "GET    /" + name + "      runs list_all" + nl
        set code to code + t + "GET    /" + name + "/:id  runs get_one" + nl
        set code to code + t + "PUT    /" + name + "/:id  runs update" + nl
        set code to code + t + "DELETE /" + name + "/:id  runs delete_one" + nl
        set code to code + t + "GET    /health        runs health" + nl

    if intent is equal "chatbot":
        set code to code + nl + "to chat with message:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "set mem to memory_new(20)" + nl
        set code to code + t + "memory_add(mem, " + q + "user" + q + ", message)" + nl
        set code to code + t + "set history to memory_summary(mem)" + nl
        set code to code + t + "ask AI to " + q + "Reply to: " + q + " + history save as reply" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "reply" + q + ": reply}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to health:" + nl + t + "respond with {" + q + "status" + q + ": " + q + "ok" + q + "}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl + t + "POST /chat runs chat" + nl + t + "GET /health runs health" + nl

    if intent is equal "classifier":
        set code to code + nl + "to classify with text:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "ask AI to " + q + "Classify: positive/negative/neutral" + q + " using text save as label" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "label" + q + ": label}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl + t + "POST /classify runs classify" + nl

    if intent is equal "summarizer":
        set code to code + nl + "to summarize with document:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "ask AI to " + q + "Summarize preserving key points" + q + " using document save as summary" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "summary" + q + ": summary}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl + t + "POST /summarize runs summarize" + nl

    if intent is equal "pipeline":
        set code to code + nl + "to process with records:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "set valid to []" + nl
        set code to code + t + "set errors to []" + nl
        set code to code + t + "repeat for each record in records:" + nl
        set code to code + t + t + "if record.id is not equal nil:" + nl
        set code to code + t + t + t + "append record to valid" + nl
        set code to code + t + t + "otherwise:" + nl
        set code to code + t + t + t + "append {" + q + "error" + q + ": " + q + "missing id" + q + "} to errors" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "processed" + q + ": len(valid), " + q + "errors" + q + ": errors}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl + t + "POST /process runs process" + nl

    if intent is equal "webhook":
        set code to code + nl + "to handle with payload:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "log " + q + "Webhook: " + q + " + string(payload.event)" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "received" + q + ": true}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl + t + "POST /webhook runs handle" + nl

    if intent is equal "finance":
        set code to code + nl + "to get_price with symbol:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "purpose: " + q + "Get stock price" + q + nl
        set code to code + t + "gather data from " + q + "https://api.example.com/price/" + q + " + symbol" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "symbol" + q + ": symbol, " + q + "price" + q + ": data.price}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to health:" + nl + t + "respond with {" + q + "status" + q + ": " + q + "ok" + q + "}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl + t + "GET /price/:symbol runs get_price" + nl + t + "GET /health runs health" + nl

    if intent is equal "monitoring":
        set code to code + nl + "to check_health:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "status" + q + ": " + q + "ok" + q + ", " + q + "time" + q + ": now()}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to get_metrics:" + nl
        set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "requests" + q + ": 0, " + q + "errors" + q + ": 0}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl + t + "GET /health runs check_health" + nl + t + "GET /metrics runs get_metrics" + nl

    if intent is equal "ncui":
        set code to "page " + q + name + q + nl
        set code to code + "theme " + q + "dark" + q + nl
        set code to code + "accent " + q + "#4F46E5" + q + nl + nl
        set code to code + "nav:" + nl + t + "brand " + q + name + q + nl
        set code to code + t + "links:" + nl + t + t + "link " + q + "Home" + q + " to " + q + "#home" + q + nl + nl
        set code to code + "section hero:" + nl + t + "heading " + q + name + q + nl
        set code to code + t + "text " + q + "Built with NC" + q + nl
        set code to code + t + "button " + q + "Start" + q + " style " + q + "primary" + q + nl + nl
        set code to code + "footer:" + nl + t + "text " + q + "Powered by NC" + q + nl

    if intent is equal "service":
        if has_ai:
            set code to code + nl + "to process with input:" + nl
            set code to code + t + "ask AI to " + q + "Process this" + q + " using input save as result" + nl
            set code to code + t + "respond with result" + nl + nl
        otherwise:
            set code to code + nl + "to handle with request:" + nl
            set code to code + t + "respond with {" + q + "message" + q + ": " + q + "Hello from " + name + q + "}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "to health:" + nl + t + "respond with {" + q + "status" + q + ": " + q + "ok" + q + "}" + nl + nl
        set code to code + "api:" + nl + t + "POST / runs handle" + nl + t + "GET /health runs health" + nl

    respond with code

// ── Main Generation ─────────────────────────────────────────

to generate with prompt:
    purpose: "Generate NC code from natural language"
    set intent_info to detect_intent(prompt)
    set code to generate_from_template(intent_info.intent, intent_info.name, intent_info.features)
    respond with {
        "code": code,
        "intent": intent_info.intent,
        "features": intent_info.features,
        "name": intent_info.name,
        "language": "nc",
        "generated_by": "NC AI v2.0"
    }

// ── Generate Project ────────────────────────────────────────

to generate_project with name, description:
    purpose: "Generate a complete NC project"
    set result to generate(description)
    set files to []
    append {"name": name + ".nc", "content": result.code} to files

    set q to chr(34)
    set nl to chr(10)
    set test_code to "service " + q + "test-" + name + q + nl + "version " + q + "1.0.0" + q + nl + nl
    set test_code to test_code + "to test_health:" + nl + "    log " + q + "Testing..." + q + nl
    set test_code to test_code + "    respond with {" + q + "passed" + q + ": true}" + nl
    append {"name": "test_" + name + ".nc", "content": test_code} to files

    respond with {"name": name, "files": files}

// ── Generate UI ─────────────────────────────────────────────

to generate_ui with description:

    respond with {"code": code, "type": "ncui"}

// ── Explain Code ────────────────────────────────────────────

// ── Convert to NC ───────────────────────────────────────────

    }

// === FILE: nc-ai/nc/training/distill.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NC AI Knowledge Distillation — Written 100% in NC
//
//  Distill knowledge from any external teacher LLM into
//  NC AI's built-in model. The teacher generates NC code,
//  the student (NC AI) learns from it.
//
//  Built by DevHeal Labs AI
//
//  Usage:
//    nc nc-ai/nc/training/distill.nc \
//      --url http://localhost:11434/v1/chat/completions \
//      --model my-model
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service "nc-distill"
version "1.0.0"

configure:
    teacher_url is env("NC_AI_URL") or ""
    teacher_model is env("NC_AI_MODEL") or ""
    teacher_key is env("NC_AI_KEY") or ""
    max_tokens is 512
    temperature is 0.7
    distill_steps is 50
    distill_lr is 0.0001

// ── NC Code Prompts for Distillation ─────────────────────

to get_distill_prompts:
    purpose: "Return diverse NC code prompts for the teacher"
    set prompts to [
        "simple rest api for managing users",
        "todo app with categories and priorities",
        "weather service that fetches forecasts",
        "blog with comments and search",
        "inventory management with stock alerts",
        "recipe app with ingredients and ratings",
        "booking system with calendar and slots",
        "notes app with tags and folders",
        "expense tracker with charts",
        "file upload service with storage",
        "contact form with email notifications",
        "url shortener with click analytics",
        "polling app with real-time votes",
        "chat app with rooms and messages",
        "fitness tracker with workout plans",
        "invoice generator with pdf export",
        "authentication service with jwt tokens",
        "dashboard with real-time metrics",
        "e-commerce cart with checkout flow",
        "notification service with push alerts",
        "search engine for documents",
        "social feed with likes and shares",
        "task queue with worker processes",
        "api gateway with rate limiting",
        "health monitoring with alerts",
        "logging service with filters",
        "config management with environments",
        "a/b testing with analytics",
        "payment processing service",
        "image gallery with upload and tags",
        "event calendar with rsvp",
        "knowledge base with categories",
        "survey builder with responses",
        "project management with boards",
        "data pipeline with transformations",
        "video streaming service",
        "geolocation service with mapping",
        "recommendation engine",
        "content moderation service",
        "multi-tenant saas backend"
    ]
    respond with prompts

// ── Teacher LLM Communication ────────────────────────────

to ask_teacher with prompt:
    purpose: "Send a prompt to the teacher LLM and get NC code back"

    set system_msg to "You are an expert NC language programmer. Generate complete, valid NC code. Use NC syntax: service, to, set, respond with, gather from, store into, api: routes, configure: block. Always include service declaration, CRUD operations, and api routes."

    set body to {
        "model": config.teacher_model,
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": system_msg},
            {"role": "user", "content": "Write NC code for: " + prompt}
        ],
        "temperature": config.temperature,
        "max_tokens": config.max_tokens
    }

    set headers to {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
    if config.teacher_key is not empty:
        set headers["Authorization"] to "Bearer " + config.teacher_key

    set response to http_post(config.teacher_url, body, headers)

    if response.status is not 200:
        log "Teacher error: " + response.status
        respond with null

    // Extract code from response
    set content to response.body.choices.0.message.content
    if content is empty:
        set content to response.body.content.0.text
    respond with content

// ── Code Validation ──────────────────────────────────────

to validate_nc_code with code:
    purpose: "Check if teacher output is valid NC code"
    if code is empty:
        respond with false
    if length(code) < 50:
        respond with false

    set score to 0
    if code contains "service \"":
        set score to score + 1
    if code contains "to " and code contains ":":
        set score to score + 1
    if code contains "respond with":
        set score to score + 1
    if code contains "set ":
        set score to score + 1
    if code contains "api:":
        set score to score + 1
    respond with score >= 2

// ── Distillation Training Step ───────────────────────────

to distill_one with prompt and teacher_code:
    purpose: "Train student model on one teacher-generated example"

    // Combine prompt + code as training pair
    set training_text to "PROMPT: " + prompt + "\nCODE:\n" + teacher_code

    // Tokenize
    set tokens to tokenize(training_text)

    // Forward pass through student model
    set logits to model_forward(tokens)

    // Compute loss (cross-entropy against teacher tokens)
    set loss to cross_entropy(logits, tokens)

    // Backward pass
    set grads to backward(loss)

    // Clip gradients
    clip_gradients(grads, 1.0)

    // Update weights (Adam optimizer)
    adam_step(grads, config.distill_lr)

    respond with loss

// ── Full Distillation Pipeline ───────────────────────────

to run_distillation:
    purpose: "Run the complete knowledge distillation pipeline"

    log "NC AI — Knowledge Distillation"
    log "Teacher: " + config.teacher_model
    log "URL: " + config.teacher_url

    if config.teacher_url is empty:
        log "Error: No teacher URL. Set NC_AI_URL or pass --url"
        respond with error "No teacher URL configured"

    // Load student model
    set student to load_model("nc_ai_model.bin")
    if student is empty:
        log "Creating new student model..."
        set student to create_model(256, 6, 8, 4096, 512)

    // Get prompts
    set prompts to get_distill_prompts()
    set total to length(prompts)
    set successful to 0
    set pairs to []

    // Iterate through prompts
    repeat for each prompt in prompts:
        set idx to index + 1
        log "[" + idx + "/" + total + "] Asking teacher: " + prompt

        // Get teacher response
        set teacher_code to ask_teacher(prompt)
        if teacher_code is empty:
            log "  Skipped (teacher returned empty)"
            continue

        // Validate
        set valid to validate_nc_code(teacher_code)
        if valid is false:
            log "  Skipped (invalid NC code)"
            continue

        // Train student on this example
        set total_loss to 0
        repeat config.distill_steps times:
            set loss to distill_one(prompt, teacher_code)
            set total_loss to total_loss + loss
        set avg_loss to total_loss / config.distill_steps

        log "  Distilled (loss: " + round(avg_loss, 2) + ")"
        set successful to successful + 1

        // Save pair
        append {prompt: prompt, code: teacher_code} to pairs

    // Save results
    save_model(student, "nc_ai_model_distilled.bin")
    log "Model saved: nc_ai_model_distilled.bin"

    // Save pairs for future training
    set pairs_file to open("nc-ai/training_data/distilled_pairs.txt", "write")
    repeat for each pair in pairs:
        write pairs_file "PROMPT: " + pair.prompt + "\n"
        write pairs_file "CODE:\n" + pair.code + "\n\n"
    close(pairs_file)

    log "Distillation complete: " + successful + "/" + total + " prompts"
    respond with {distilled: successful, total: total, model: "nc_ai_model_distilled.bin"}

// ── API Routes ───────────────────────────────────────────

api:
    POST /distill    runs run_distillation

// === FILE: nc-ai/nc/training/learn.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NC AI Self-Learning — Written 100% in NC
//
//  Learn from existing NC projects, error-fix pairs,
//  and user-generated code. NC AI continuously improves
//  by absorbing patterns from real-world NC code.
//
//  Built by DevHeal Labs AI
//
//  Usage:
//    nc nc-ai/nc/training/learn.nc --project /path/to/project
//    nc nc-ai/nc/training/learn.nc --fixes error_log.txt
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service "nc-learn"
version "1.0.0"

configure:
    learn_lr is 0.00005
    steps_per_file is 20
    max_files is 128

// ── File Scanner ─────────────────────────────────────────

to scan_nc_files with directory:
    purpose: "Recursively find all .nc and .ncui files in a directory"
    set files to []
    set entries to list_dir(directory)

    repeat for each entry in entries:
        if entry starts with ".":
            continue
        set path to directory + "/" + entry
        if is_directory(path):
            set sub_files to scan_nc_files(path)
            repeat for each f in sub_files:
                append f to files
        if entry ends with ".nc" or entry ends with ".ncui":
            append path to files

    respond with files

// ── Learn from Project ───────────────────────────────────

to learn_from_project with project_dir:
    purpose: "Train NC AI on all NC code in a project directory"

    log "NC AI — Learning from Project"
    log "Directory: " + project_dir

    // Find all NC files
    set files to scan_nc_files(project_dir)
    set count to length(files)

    if count is 0:
        log "No .nc or .ncui files found in " + project_dir
        respond with {learned: 0}

    log "Found " + count + " files"

    // Load model
    set model to load_model("nc_ai_model.bin")
    if model is empty:
        set model to load_model("nc_ai_model_prod.bin")
    if model is empty:
        log "Error: No model found. Run nc ai train first."
        respond with error "No model found"

    // Train on each file with low learning rate
    set total_loss to 0
    repeat for each filepath in files:
        set content to read_file(filepath)
        if content is empty:
            continue

        set tokens to tokenize(content)
        set steps to config.steps_per_file

        repeat steps times:
            set logits to model_forward(tokens)
            set loss to cross_entropy(logits, tokens)
            set grads to backward(loss)
            clip_gradients(grads, 1.0)
            adam_step(grads, config.learn_lr)
            set total_loss to total_loss + loss

        log "  Learned: " + filepath

    // Save updated model
    save_model(model, "nc_ai_model_prod.bin")
    set avg_loss to total_loss / (count * config.steps_per_file)
    log "Learned from " + count + " files (avg loss: " + round(avg_loss, 2) + ")"
    respond with {learned: count, avg_loss: avg_loss}

// ── Learn from Error-Fix Pairs ───────────────────────────

to learn_from_fixes with error_log_path:
    purpose: "Train NC AI on error→fix pairs to improve auto-repair"

    log "NC AI — Learning from Error Fixes"
    log "Source: " + error_log_path

    set content to read_file(error_log_path)
    if content is empty:
        log "Error log is empty or not found"
        respond with {learned: 0}

    // Parse error→fix pairs
    set pairs to []
    set lines to split(content, "\n")
    set current_error to ""
    set current_fix to ""
    set in_fix to false

    repeat for each line in lines:
        if line starts with "ERROR:":
            if current_error is not empty and current_fix is not empty:
                append {error: current_error, fix: current_fix} to pairs
            set current_error to trim(replace(line, "ERROR:", ""))
            set current_fix to ""
            set in_fix to false
        if line starts with "FIX:":
            set in_fix to true
            set current_fix to trim(replace(line, "FIX:", ""))
        if in_fix is true and line does not start with "ERROR:" and line does not start with "FIX:":
            set current_fix to current_fix + "\n" + line

    // Add last pair
    if current_error is not empty and current_fix is not empty:
        append {error: current_error, fix: current_fix} to pairs

    set count to length(pairs)
    log "Found " + count + " error-fix pairs"

    // Load model
    set model to load_model("nc_ai_model.bin")
    if model is empty:
        log "Error: No model found"
        respond with error "No model found"

    // Train on fixes (higher LR for error patterns)
    repeat for each pair in pairs:
        set training_text to "ERROR: " + pair.error + "\nFIX:\n" + pair.fix
        set tokens to tokenize(training_text)

        repeat 30 times:
            set logits to model_forward(tokens)
            set loss to cross_entropy(logits, tokens)
            set grads to backward(loss)
            adam_step(grads, 0.0001)

        log "  Learned fix: " + truncate(pair.error, 60)

    save_model(model, "nc_ai_model_prod.bin")
    log "Learned from " + count + " fixes"
    respond with {learned: count}

// ── Auto-Learn After Create ──────────────────────────────

to auto_learn with prompt and generated_code:
    purpose: "Automatically learn from each nc ai create command"

    // Save to training corpus
    set corpus_path to home_dir() + "/.nc/training_corpus.txt"
    set f to open(corpus_path, "append")
    write f generated_code + "\n"
    close(f)

    // Save prompt-code pair
    set pairs_path to "nc-ai/training_data/prompt_pairs.txt"
    set f to open(pairs_path, "append")
    write f "\nPROMPT: " + prompt + "\n"
    write f "CODE:\n" + generated_code + "\n"
    close(f)

    log "Self-learn: saved prompt-code pair"
    respond with true

// ── API Routes ───────────────────────────────────────────

api:
    POST /learn/project    runs learn_from_project
    POST /learn/fixes      runs learn_from_fixes
    POST /learn/auto       runs auto_learn

// === FILE: nc-ai/nc/training/train.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NC AI Training Pipeline — Written 100% in NC Language
//
//  Self-contained training script that includes tokenizer,
//  transformer, and training logic in one file.
//
//  Usage:
//    nc nc-ai/nc/training/train.nc
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

service "nc-trainer"
version "2.0.0"

configure:
    data_dir is "./nc-ai/training_data"
    model_dir is "./nc-ai/model"

// ── Build Vocabulary ────────────────────────────────────────

to build_vocab with corpus_texts:
    purpose: "Build vocabulary from NC source texts"
    set vocab to {"<PAD>": 0, "<BOS>": 1, "<EOS>": 2, "<UNK>": 3}
    set vocab_size to 4
    set keywords to ["service", "version", "configure", "to", "with", "purpose", "set", "ask", "AI", "save", "as", "respond", "if", "is", "above", "below", "equal", "not", "otherwise", "repeat", "for", "each", "in", "while", "times", "append", "run", "result", "define", "api", "GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE", "runs", "try", "on", "error", "finally", "log", "len", "get", "type", "and", "or", "true", "false", "nil", "nothing", "import", "from", "store", "gather", "into", "where", "respond with", "set ", "to ", "if ", "repeat ", "for each", "is equal", "is above", "is below", "is not", "append ", "ask AI", "api:", "runs ", "purpose:"]
    repeat for each kw in keywords:
        if get(vocab, kw) is equal nil:
            set vocab[kw] to vocab_size
            set vocab_size to vocab_size + 1
    set patterns to [": ", ", ", ". ", "  ", "    ", "{", "}", "[", "]", "(", ")", "+", "-", "*", "/", "=", ":", " ", "\n", "\"", "'", "_", "//"]
    repeat for each pat in patterns:
        if get(vocab, pat) is equal nil:
            set vocab[pat] to vocab_size
            set vocab_size to vocab_size + 1
    set chars to "abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789"
    set ci to 0
    repeat while ci is below len(chars):
        set ch to substr(chars, ci, 1)
        if get(vocab, ch) is equal nil:
            set vocab[ch] to vocab_size
            set vocab_size to vocab_size + 1
        set ci to ci + 1
    log "Vocabulary: " + string(vocab_size) + " tokens"
    respond with vocab_size

// ── Encode ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

to encode with text:
    purpose: "Encode text to token IDs"
    set tokens to [1]
    set i to 0
    repeat while i is below len(text):
        set best_len to 0
        set try_len to 15
        if try_len is above len(text) - i:
            set try_len to len(text) - i
        repeat while try_len is above 0:
            set window to substr(text, i, try_len)
            set tid to get(vocab, window)
            if tid is not equal nil:
                set best_len to try_len
                set try_len to 0
            otherwise:
                set try_len to try_len - 1
        if best_len is above 0:
            set window to substr(text, i, best_len)
            append get(vocab, window) to tokens
            set i to i + best_len
        otherwise:
            set ch to substr(text, i, 1)
            set tid to get(vocab, ch)
            if tid is not equal nil:
                append tid to tokens
            otherwise:
                append 3 to tokens
            set i to i + 1
    append 2 to tokens
    respond with tokens

// ── Decode ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

to decode with token_ids:
    purpose: "Decode token IDs to text"
    set parts to []
    set rev to {}
    repeat for each entry in vocab:
        set rev[string(entry.value)] to entry.key
    repeat for each tid in token_ids:
        if tid is not equal 0:
            if tid is not equal 1:
                if tid is not equal 2:
                    set s to get(rev, string(tid))
                    if s is not equal nil:
                        append s to parts
    respond with join(parts, "")

// ── Initialize Transformer ──────────────────────────────────

to init_model with config:
    purpose: "Initialize transformer"
    log "Init model: " + string(config.embed_dim) + "d, " + string(config.num_layers) + " layers"
    set model_config to config
    set token_embedding to tensor_random(config.vocab_size, config.embed_dim)
    set pos_embedding to tensor_random(config.max_seq_len, config.embed_dim)
    set layers to []
    set li to 0
    repeat while li is below config.num_layers:
        set layer to {"qw": tensor_random(config.embed_dim, config.embed_dim), "kw": tensor_random(config.embed_dim, config.embed_dim), "vw": tensor_random(config.embed_dim, config.embed_dim), "ow": tensor_random(config.embed_dim, config.embed_dim), "ng": tensor_ones(1, config.embed_dim), "nb": tensor_create(1, config.embed_dim), "uw": tensor_random(config.embed_dim, config.ff_dim), "dw": tensor_random(config.ff_dim, config.embed_dim), "fg": tensor_ones(1, config.embed_dim), "fb": tensor_create(1, config.embed_dim)}
        append layer to layers
        set li to li + 1
    set final_ng to tensor_ones(1, config.embed_dim)
    set final_nb to tensor_create(1, config.embed_dim)
    set lm_head to tensor_random(config.embed_dim, config.vocab_size)
    log "Model ready"
    respond with true

// ── Forward Pass ────────────────────────────────────────────

to forward with token_ids:
    purpose: "Transformer forward pass"
    set seq_len to len(token_ids)
    set x to tensor_embedding(token_embedding, token_ids)
    set pos_ids to []
    set i to 0
    repeat while i is below seq_len:
        append i to pos_ids
        set i to i + 1
    set pe to tensor_embedding(pos_embedding, pos_ids)
    set x to tensor_add(x, pe)
    set li to 0
    repeat while li is below model_config.num_layers:
        set L to layers[li]
        set n to tensor_layer_norm(x, L.ng, L.nb)
        set Q to tensor_matmul(n, L.qw)
        set K to tensor_matmul(n, L.kw)
        set V to tensor_matmul(n, L.vw)
        set KT to tensor_transpose(K)
        set sc to tensor_matmul(Q, KT)
        set dk to model_config.embed_dim / model_config.num_heads
        set sc to tensor_scale(sc, 1.0 / sqrt(dk))
        set mask to tensor_causal_mask(seq_len)
        set sc to tensor_add(sc, mask)
        set w to tensor_softmax(sc)
        set ctx to tensor_matmul(w, V)
        set o to tensor_matmul(ctx, L.ow)
        set x to tensor_add(x, o)
        set n2 to tensor_layer_norm(x, L.fg, L.fb)
        set h to tensor_matmul(n2, L.uw)
        set h to tensor_gelu(h)
        set h to tensor_matmul(h, L.dw)
        set x to tensor_add(x, h)
        set li to li + 1
    set x to tensor_layer_norm(x, final_ng, final_nb)
    set logits to tensor_matmul(x, lm_head)
    respond with logits

// ── Compute Loss ────────────────────────────────────────────

to compute_loss with token_batch, target_batch:
    purpose: "Cross-entropy loss on batch"
    set total to 0
    set bs to len(token_batch)
    set i to 0
    repeat while i is below bs:
        set logits to forward(token_batch[i])
        set loss to tensor_cross_entropy(logits, target_batch[i])
        set total to total + loss
        set i to i + 1
    respond with total / bs

// ── Prepare Batch ───────────────────────────────────────────

to prepare_batch with pairs, bs, max_len:
    purpose: "Tokenize and prepare batch"
    set inp to []
    set tgt to []
    set i to 0
    repeat while i is below bs:
        if i is below len(pairs):
            set pair to pairs[i]
            set tokens to encode(pair.prompt + " => " + pair.code)
            if len(tokens) is above max_len:
                set tokens to slice(tokens, 0, max_len)
            append slice(tokens, 0, len(tokens) - 1) to inp
            append slice(tokens, 1, len(tokens)) to tgt
        set i to i + 1
    respond with {"inputs": inp, "targets": tgt}

// ── Train Epoch ─────────────────────────────────────────────

to train_epoch with train_pairs, bs, max_len, step:
    purpose: "Train one epoch"
    set epoch_loss to 0
    set batches to 0
    set pos to 0
    repeat while pos is below len(train_pairs):
        set end to min(pos + bs, len(train_pairs))
        set batch to prepare_batch(slice(train_pairs, pos, end), end - pos, max_len)
        set loss to compute_loss(batch.inputs, batch.targets)
        set epoch_loss to epoch_loss + loss
        set batches to batches + 1
        set step to step + 1
        set pos to end
    respond with {"loss": epoch_loss / batches, "step": step}

// ── Save Model ──────────────────────────────────────────────

to save_model with path:
    purpose: "Save model weights"
    tensor_save(token_embedding, path + "/token_emb.nct")
    tensor_save(pos_embedding, path + "/pos_emb.nct")
    tensor_save(lm_head, path + "/lm_head.nct")
    tensor_save(final_ng, path + "/final_ng.nct")
    tensor_save(final_nb, path + "/final_nb.nct")
    set li to 0
    repeat while li is below model_config.num_layers:
        set L to layers[li]
        set p to path + "/layer_" + string(li)
        tensor_save(L.qw, p + "_qw.nct")
        tensor_save(L.kw, p + "_kw.nct")
        tensor_save(L.vw, p + "_vw.nct")
        tensor_save(L.ow, p + "_ow.nct")
        tensor_save(L.ng, p + "_ng.nct")
        tensor_save(L.nb, p + "_nb.nct")
        tensor_save(L.uw, p + "_uw.nct")
        tensor_save(L.dw, p + "_dw.nct")
        tensor_save(L.fg, p + "_fg.nct")
        tensor_save(L.fb, p + "_fb.nct")
        set li to li + 1
    set cfg_json to json_encode(model_config)
    write_file(path + "/config.json", cfg_json)
    set vocab_json to json_encode(vocab)
    write_file(path + "/vocab.json", vocab_json)
    log "Model saved to " + string(path)
    respond with true

// ── Main ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

to main:
    purpose: "Train NC AI model"
    log "══════════════════════════════════════════"
    log "  NC AI Training — 100% NC Language"
    log "══════════════════════════════════════════"
    log ""
    set data_dir to "./nc-ai/training_data"
    set model_dir to "./nc-ai/model"
    log "Loading training data..."
    set raw to read_file(data_dir + "/training_pairs.json")
    if raw is equal nil:
        log "No training data found!"
        respond with false
    set all_pairs to json_decode(raw)
    log "Loaded " + string(len(all_pairs)) + " training pairs"
    log ""
    log "Building tokenizer..."
    set corpus to []
    repeat for each pair in all_pairs:
        append pair.code to corpus
    set vsize to build_vocab(corpus)
    log ""
    log "Initializing model..."
    set cfg to {"vocab_size": vsize, "embed_dim": 64, "num_heads": 4, "num_layers": 2, "ff_dim": 256, "max_seq_len": 64}
    init_model(cfg)
    log ""
    set split to floor(len(all_pairs) * 0.9)
    set train_pairs to slice(all_pairs, 0, split)
    log "Training on " + string(len(train_pairs)) + " examples..."
    log ""
    set step to 0
    set best to 999999
    set ep to 0
    repeat while ep is below 3:
        log "Epoch " + string(ep + 1) + "/3"
        set r to train_epoch(train_pairs, 4, 64, step)
        set step to r.step
        log "  Loss: " + string(round(r.loss, 4))
        if r.loss is below best:
            set best to r.loss
            save_model(model_dir)
            log "  Saved (best)"
        set ep to ep + 1
    log ""
    log "Training complete! Best loss: " + string(round(best, 4))
    respond with {"best_loss": best, "steps": step}

api:
    POST /train runs main

to test_export_package_manifest:
    purpose: "Package export should create package.nc"
    set dir to "/tmp/test_pkg_" + str(now())
    mkdir(dir)
    write_file(dir + "/service.nc", "service \"test\"\n")

    export_package(dir)

    assert file_exists(dir + "/package.nc"), "Should create package.nc"
    set manifest to read_file(dir + "/package.nc")
    assert manifest contains "package", "Should have package declaration"
    assert manifest contains "version", "Should have version"

    remove_dir(dir)
    respond with "ok"

to test_export_readme_generated:
    purpose: "ZIP export should generate README"
    set dir to "/tmp/test_zip_" + str(now())
    mkdir(dir)
    write_file(dir + "/service.nc", "service \"test\"\n")

    export_zip(dir)

    assert file_exists(dir + "/README.md"), "Should create README"
    set readme to read_file(dir + "/README.md")
    assert readme contains "NC Language", "README should reference NC"
    assert readme contains "DevHeal Labs AI", "README should credit DevHeal"

    remove_dir(dir)
    respond with "ok"

to run_all_tests:

    set tests to [
        "test_scan_project",
        "test_scan_project_categorizes",
        "test_export_docker_generates",
        "test_export_package_manifest",
        "test_export_readme_generated"
    ]

    set passed to 0
    set failed to 0

    repeat for each test in tests:
        log "  Running: " + test
        set result to call(test)
        if result is "ok":
            log "    PASS"
            set passed to passed + 1
        else:

            set failed to failed + 1

// === FILE: nc-ai/tests/test_ai_recommend.nc ===
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  NC AI Test Suite — Code Recommendations
//  Tests nc ai review functionality
//
//  Run: nc run nc-ai/tests/test_ai_recommend.nc
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to test_recommend_missing_health:
    purpose: "Should recommend health endpoint"
    set code to "service \"test\"\nversion \"1.0.0\"\nto list:\n    respond with []\napi:\n    GET /items runs list\n"
    set recs to analyze_service(code)
    set found to false
    repeat for each r in recs:
        if r.msg contains "health":
            set found to true
    assert found is true, "Should recommend health endpoint"
    respond with "ok"

to test_recommend_middleware:
    purpose: "Should recommend middleware"
    set code to "service \"test\"\nversion \"1.0.0\"\nto hello:\n    respond with \"ok\"\napi:\n    GET / runs hello\n"
    set recs to analyze_service(code)
    set found to false
    repeat for each r in recs:
        if r.msg contains "middleware":
            set found to true
    assert found is true, "Should recommend middleware"
    respond with "ok"

to test_recommend_id_generation:
    purpose: "Should recommend generate_id for store operations"
    set code to "service \"test\"\nto create with data:\n    store data into \"items\"\n    respond with data\napi:\n    POST /items runs create\n"
    set recs to analyze_service(code)
    set found to false
    repeat for each r in recs:
        if r.msg contains "generate_id":
            set found to true
    assert found is true, "Should recommend generate_id()"
    respond with "ok"

to test_recommend_auth_for_users:
    purpose: "Should recommend auth for user-facing services"
    set code to "service \"user-api\"\nto list_users:\n    gather items from \"users\"\n    respond with items\napi:\n    GET /users runs list_users\n"
    set recs to analyze_service(code)
    set found to false
    repeat for each r in recs:
        if r.msg contains "auth":
            set found to true
    assert found is true, "Should recommend auth for user service"
    respond with "ok"

to test_clean_code_high_score:
    purpose: "Well-written code should get high score"
    set code to "service \"test-api\"\nversion \"1.0.0\"\n\nconfigure:\n    port is 8000\n\nmiddleware:\n    use cors\n    use log_requests\n\nto list_items:\n    gather items from \"items\"\n    respond with items\n\nto create_item with data:\n    set data.id to generate_id()\n    set data.created_at to now()\n    store data into \"items\"\n    log \"Created: \" + data.id\n    respond with data\n\nto health_check:\n    respond with {status: \"healthy\"}\n\napi:\n    GET /items runs list_items\n    POST /items runs create_item\n    GET /health runs health_check\n"
    set result to review_code(code)
    assert result.score >= 85, "Clean code should score 85+"
    respond with "ok"

to test_ncui_recommendations:
    purpose: "Should recommend data binding for static pages"
    set code to "page \"Test\"\n\nsection hero:\n    heading \"Hello\"\n    text \"World\"\n"
    set recs to analyze_page(code)
    set found_data to false
    repeat for each r in recs:
        if r.msg contains "data":
            set found_data to true
    assert found_data is true, "Should recommend data binding"
    respond with "ok"

        "test_recommend_id_generation",

// === FILE: nc-ai/train_nc_model.nc ===
to main:
    show "NC AI Model — Full Ecosystem Training (BLAS-accelerated)"
    show "Powered by DevHeal Labs AI"
    show ""

    set config to {"dim": 256, "n_layers": 6, "n_heads": 8, "vocab_size": 4096, "max_seq": 512, "hidden_dim": 1024}
    show "Model: dim=256, 6 layers, 8 heads, 4096 vocab, 512 context"
    set model to nc_model_create(config)
    show "Model created!"

    // Full NC ecosystem corpus — 278K+ lines covering everything
    set data_files to ["training_data/nc_corpus/nc_engine_full.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_lang_all_nc.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_ui_complete.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/hiveant_complete.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/swarmops_complete.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_ai_engine.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_ai_modules.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_ai_native.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_ai_tests.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_ai_prompts.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_apps_complete.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_scripts_complete.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/neuraledge_complete.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/all_documentation.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/all_websites.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/all_scripts.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_lang_docs.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_lang_js.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_lang_configs.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_lang_templates.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/patent_docs.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/devheallabs.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_engine_internals.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc_ui_full.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/all_nc_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc-lang_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/hiveant_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/swarmops_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc-ui_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc-ai_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc-scripts_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/nc-apps_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/neuraledge_code.txt", "training_data/nc_corpus/user_generated.txt"]

    set train_config to {"lr": 0.0003, "batch_size": 4, "steps": 5000, "checkpoint_dir": "training_data/checkpoints"}

    show "Training on 34 corpus files (278K+ lines) | 5000 steps | lr=0.0003"
    show ""
    set result to nc_model_train(data_files, train_config)
    show ""
    show "Training done:"
    show result

    nc_model_save("nc_ai_model_prod.bin")
    show "Saved: nc_ai_model_prod.bin"

    show ""
    show "Testing generation..."
    set code to nc_model_generate_text("to hello:", 100, 0.7)
    show "Generated:"
    show code

    show ""
    show "NC AI Full Ecosystem Training Complete!"
